# Current Starshine `optimize-instructions` strategy

## Fresh aggregate consumer boundaries

Binaryen v130's `visitStructGet` does not inspect `struct.new` or `struct.new_default`; it only handles null/cast and memory-order concerns. Starshine therefore preserves ordinary, packed, default, and effectful fresh-struct reads. The stale direct field-forwarding rule and its packed/default-value and selected-operand localization fact surface are deleted rather than retained as a producer-shape matrix.

## Fresh repeated-array consumer boundary

Binaryen v130 keeps `array.get`, `array.set`, and `array.len` over every fresh `array.new`, `array.new_fixed`, and `array.new_default` producer; those visitors do not prove or localize constructor operands. Starshine therefore limits represented fresh-array rules to constructor canonicalization such as size-one `array.new` to `array.new_fixed` and repeated fixed values to repeated/default constructors. Consumer rewrites no longer infer fresh-array results, erase writes, or replace out-of-bounds operations with localized effects and `unreachable`. This is one source-backed producer/consumer boundary, not a profile-shape matrix. Removing the stale consumer rules also deletes their array pack/default, allocation trap-budget, ordered-void, and nop helper debt.

## Width-specific masks and literal ordering

Redundant low-ones mask removal follows Binaryen v130's width-specific ownership: the represented rule applies to i32 only; i64 masks remain explicit even when reusable maxBits facts prove them redundant. Generic commutative canonicalization also ranks literal leaves after unary/conversion, binary, and compare expressions, keeping mask constants on the right without weakening the existing effect/order swap proof.

## Syntactic `call_ref` target proof

Directization follows Binaryen v130's syntactic target fallthrough only: direct `ref.func`, supported wrappers, table targets, and select targets remain candidate families, but an earlier `ref.func` assignment does not prove a later `local.get` target. The raw local-use-count bridge and its local-fallthrough admission state are deleted. `RawOiCurrentRootRevisionOverlay` remains a current-root plus immutable-region discovery view and cannot substitute local dataflow for exact target proof.

## Known-result reference-test preservation

Known `ref.test` success and failure now use one general typed preservation rule: retain the tested operand under `drop`, then materialize the i32 constant. This directly follows Binaryen v130 `visitRefTest` and applies to ordinary and descriptor tests, including pure direct nulls and local reads. Candidate/type relation facts may prove the result, but purity no longer authorizes deleting the explicit operand; the former effect/erasure matrix and direct-constant plan are removed.

This page is the local strategy overview.
For the exact helper walk and finer-grained code map, use [`./starshine-hot-ir-strategy.md`](./starshine-hot-ir-strategy.md).

## Short version

The active OI architecture migration is fact-driven: candidate roots and immutable raw regions only discover work, while family facts continue to prove exact types, equality, effects, removability, evaluation order, traps, and invalidation. The descriptor stack bridge now has a reusable per-revision `RawOiDescriptorCallValueGraphFact`; the dispatcher shares it across descriptor families and rebuilds only after mutation. Balanced local direct-call exact-success/miss, direct-call exactification, both-direct-call miss, and local-operand miss families query its preclassified local, nontrapping-leaf, exactification, and rich typed chunk runs plus syntactic direct/call_ref/table producer endpoints instead of scanning independently. Scalar `local.tee`, pure select, trapping div/rem, parameterized scalar/reference calls, branch-free value blocks, no-parameter calls, and leaf chunks are graph facts; exact descriptor signatures, target/subtype, arity, order, effects, traps, and rewrite legality remain family-owned. This does not widen the transforms. The final escaping-label `ref.get_desc` bridge is also candidate-driven now: one immutable region per recursive body identifies only `block` plus optional `ref.as_non_null`, `ref.get_desc`, and `ref.cast_desc_eq` envelopes. Exact branch payload/fallthrough typing, label retargeting, descriptor result type, effects, traps, source order, and rewrite emission stay in `RawOiEscapingRefGetDescFlattenFact`. The prefix value graph is intentionally not reused as semantic proof because branch-free prefix hoisting cannot establish escaping branch-target decrements.

Current Starshine `src/passes/optimize_instructions.mbt` is a real HOT pass, but it is still narrower than Binaryen `OptimizeInstructions.cpp`. The `[O4Z-AUDIT-OI-A]` `version_130` matrix now makes that gap actionable by assigning each upstream source/lit family to current coverage, an explicit local boundary, or a follow-up slice.

`OiRefIsNullResultFact` follows Binaryen v130's direct result rule rather than generic known-null folding: proven non-nullability yields zero, while direct or dataflow-known null values keep the predicate. Known-null facts remain reusable for trap-producing casts, descriptor operations, and other families that explicitly consume them.

The reusable sign-width facts deliberately distinguish signed producers from literal knowledge: redundant sign extensions may be removed after signed loads/extension producers or compatible local producer facts, but direct literals and literal local assignments keep their extension shells to match Binaryen v130's direct pass output. This is one general producer-kind boundary, not a profile-case whitelist.

The implemented center of gravity is:

- exact binary constant folding through `OiI32ExactConstBinaryFact` / `OiI64ExactConstBinaryFact` and constant integer `eq` / `ne` compare folding
- non-constant `eqz` / compare-to-zero rewrites, same-local integer compare and binary operand folding through `OiSameLocalIntegerCompareFact` and `OiSameLocalIntegerBinaryFact`, endpoint unsigned-domain compare folds through `OiUnsignedDomainEdgeCompareFact` (`x <_u 0`, `x >=_u 0`, `x >_u UINT_MAX`, `x <=_u UINT_MAX`) with effect preservation, side-effect-free signed-domain endpoint folds through `OiSignedDomainEdgeCompareFact` (`x <s INT_MIN`, `x >=s INT_MIN`, `x >s INT_MAX`, `x <=s INT_MAX`) with effectful signed endpoint compares intentionally kept to match the oracle boundary, pure and effect-preserving i32/i64 masked unsigned-compare folds plus first pure/effect-preserving i32/i64 `shr_u` bounded unsigned-compare folds, first straight-line local-carried, `i32.wrap_i64`, and `i64.extend_i32_u` unsigned max facts including narrowed child facts, first direct nonnegative signed-relational folds and signed-to-unsigned compare spellings, signed zero-lhs constant relational folds, signed zero-rhs constant relational keep/canonicalize boundary coverage, and relational constant canonicalization
- commutative operand ordering with HOT use-def safety guards
- add/sub/mul/shift rewrites, including constant shift/rotate effective-amount masking (`31`/`63`) through existing constant-fold/identity machinery
- constant-`if` folding and constant-condition / identical-pure-arm local/global/ref.null/ref.func/ref.i31 (including narrow same-order `i32.add(local.get, i32.const)`, `i32.sub(local.get, i32.const)`, `i32.mul(local.get, i32.const)`, `i32.and(local.get, i32.const)`, `i32.or(local.get, i32.const)`, `i32.xor(local.get, i32.const)`, `i32.shl(local.get, i32.const)`, `i32.shr_u(local.get, `i32.popcnt(local.get)`, `i32.extend8_s(local.get)`, `i32.extend16_s(local.get)`, direct `i32.trunc_sat_f32_*` / `i32.trunc_sat_f64_*`, direct `i32.reinterpret_f32`, direct `i32.wrap_i64`, and same-order direct `i32.div_s` / `i32.div_u` / `i32.rem_s` / `i32.rem_u(local.get, i32.const)` payload shells)/integer/float `select` cleanup, plus direct same-order `i32`/`i64` local/constant numeric local.get)` / `i32.shr_u(local.get, local.get)` / `i32.rotl(local.get, local.get)` / `i32.rotr(local.get, local.get)` / `i64.add(local.get, local.get)` / `i64.mul(local.get, local.get)` / local.get)` / `i64.shr_u(local.get, local.get)` / `i64.rotl(local.get, local.get)` / `i64.rotr(local.get, local.get)` same-ordered-local shells plus direct i32/i64 and f32/f64 compare same-ordered-local shells and direct f32/f64 binary same-ordered-local shells, and effectful-condition identical-arm cleanup for direct leaves plus the nontrapping same-ordered `i32.add(local.get, local.get)`, `i64.add(local.get, local.get)`, `i32.sub(local.get, local.get)`, `i64.sub(local.get, local.get)`, `i32.mul(local.get, local.get)`, `i64.mul(local.get, local.get)`, `i32.and(local.get, local.get)`, `i32.or(local.get, local.get)`, `i32.xor(local.get, local.get)`, `i64.and(local.get, local.get)`, `i64.or(local.get, local.get)`, `i64.xor(local.get, local.get)`, i32/i64 shift, i32/i64 module context; mutable `global.get` arms remain side-effect-free-condition only and are not moved across effectful conditions
- nested boolean-`if` normalization, `eqz` wrapping, boolean constant tree leaves selected by `OiBooleanConstantLeafKind` plus single-result `if` payload outcomes selected by `OiBooleanConstantIfPayloadKind` through `OiBooleanConstantLeafFact` / `OiBooleanConstantIfPayloadFact`, unshared nested boolean-condition leaves selected by `OiBooleanTreeLeafKind` plus single-use single-result `if` payload outcomes selected by `OiBooleanTreeIfPayloadKind` through `OiBooleanTreeLeafFact` / `OiBooleanTreeIfPayloadFact`, the narrow direct De Morgan `i32.and(i32.eqz X, i32.eqz Y)` to `i32.eqz(i32.or X Y)` cleanup through `OiDeMorganAndEqzFact`, exact i32 `1/0` and `0/1` boolean select-arm classification through shared `OiI32BooleanSelectArmFact`, direct boolean constant `select` cleanup through `OiBooleanConstSelectFact`, direct `i32.eqz` select-condition cleanup by swapping select arms, direct `i32.eqz(compare)` boolean-select cleanup, and direct `i64.eqz` boolean-select cleanup through `OiEqzConditionSelectFact`, direct i32/i64 `eq` / `ne` zero select-condition cleanup by dropping the redundant compare through `OiZeroCompareConditionSelectFact` and nested `OiZeroCompareConditionCompareFact`, direct i32/i64 `eq` / `ne` boolean-select cleanup through `OiIntegerEqualityConditionSelectFact`, plus direct integer-relational and float equality/inequality boolean-select cleanup through `OiDirectCompareConditionSelectFact` while leaving non-boolean i64.eqz value selects unchanged
- duplicate-branch collapse in then-regions through `OiDirectBranchRootFact` roots and `OiBranchPairRelationKind`-selected same-label/arity/operand facts
- the OI-J direct-call exact descriptor-miss family under semantic preconditions: ordered nontrapping `local.get*`, scalar constant (`i32.const`/`i64.const` with the shared scanner predicate also covering `f32.const`/`f64.const`), or `global.get` ref args; direct strict-subtype ref call; ordered nontrapping `local.get*`, scalar constant, or `global.get` descriptor args; direct exact-descriptor call; and source-order-preserving call/drop/unreachable output
- the sibling OI-J pure-reference/direct-descriptor-call or exact `ref.func` + `call_ref` descriptor-producer exact descriptor-miss family under semantic preconditions: pure strict-subtype `local.get` reference operand, or a direct strict-subtype reference call for the call_ref descriptor-producer subset; ordered nontrapping `local.get*`, scalar constant (`i32.const`/`i64.const` with the shared scanner predicate also covering `f32.const`/`f64.const`), `global.get`, branch-free value-block descriptor-call args, no-parameter direct value-call descriptor-call args, parameterized direct value-call descriptor-call args with ordered nontrapping leaf operands, no-parameter direct non-null reference-result descriptor-call args, parameterized direct non-null reference-result descriptor-call args with ordered nontrapping leaf operands, scalar-producer `local.tee` descriptor-call args, pure nontrapping-leaf `select` descriptor-call args, or stack-form trapping integer div/rem scalar descriptor-call args with nontrapping leaves; direct descriptor call with matching parameter count and exact target descriptor result, or `ref.func` plus `call_ref` whose direct target and static call_ref type both return an exact non-null descriptor for the cast target with matching parameter count; and source-order-preserving `desc args; call desc; drop; unreachable` output
- the sibling OI-J pure-local direct-call exact descriptor-success family under semantic preconditions: ordered `local.get*` ref args, direct exact non-null target ref call, ordered `local.get*` descriptor args, direct exact target descriptor call, and source-order-preserving `ref args; call ref; desc args; call desc; drop` output; exact-success casts with scalar-constant or `global.get` direct-call arguments are a Binaryen-backed keep-spelling boundary, not part of the broader nontrapping-argument exactification/miss predicates
- the OI-J TNH typed-table `call_ref` exact descriptor-success families under semantic preconditions: after call_ref directization, ordered nontrapping leaf operands plus a nontrapping table index feed either a reference-side `call_indirect` whose type returns an exact non-null target reference paired with a direct descriptor call, or a descriptor-side `call_indirect` whose type returns an exact non-null descriptor paired with a direct exact reference call; default and IIT keep the exact descriptor cast, while `--traps-never-happen` preserves source order and drops the descriptor result without the descriptor equality trap
- the adjacent OI-J direct-call descriptor exactification/narrowing family under semantic preconditions: ordered nontrapping `local.get*`, scalar constant (`i32.const`/`i64.const` with the same scanner predicate covering `f32.const`/`f64.const`), `global.get`, or no-parameter direct scalar value-call chunks as ref-call args, direct same-heap non-null ref call, ordered nontrapping `local.get*`, scalar constant, `global.get`, or no-parameter direct scalar value-call chunks as descriptor-call args, direct exact target descriptor call, and source-order-preserving `ref.cast_desc_eq` retention that rebuilds inexact or nullable source casts as non-null exact without skipping the descriptor check
- the OI-J standalone `ref.get_desc` null-check movement family for direct locals, nullable global.get leaves, local.tee chunks fed by nontrapping nullable local/global leaves, branch-free blocks, self-contained branch/cast blocks, escaping direct-`br` and value-`br_table` block children, branch-free select/effect-safe if nullable children, and direct-call and typed-table-call_ref/directized `call_indirect` children with no parameters or nontrapping leaf operands, preserving the nullable child as the `ref.get_desc` operand in default/TNH-focused tests; plus the distinct standalone known-null trap-producing family for direct `ref.null`, `local.tee(ref.null)`, and branch-free blocks ending in `ref.null`, which rewrites to unreachable-producing shapes instead of moving the child under `ref.get_desc`
- dead-region-suffix cleanup with explicit fallback-branch and zero-sentinel preservation

That is a meaningful implemented pass.
But it is not yet the full upstream AST surface.

## Exact local code map

| Surface | Exact code location |
| --- | --- |
| registry descriptor and public summary | `src/passes/optimize.mbt:189-191` |
| hot-preset placement | `src/passes/optimize.mbt:288-303`, `src/passes/optimize.mbt:442-461` |
| hot-pipeline dispatch | `src/passes/pass_manager.mbt:8989` |
| owner file and main entry | `src/passes/optimize_instructions.mbt:2-16`, `src/passes/optimize_instructions.mbt:30-31`, `src/passes/optimize_instructions.mbt:3239-3248` |
| focused reduced-pass tests | `src/passes/optimize_instructions_test.mbt:2`, `src/passes/optimize_instructions_test.mbt:83`, `src/passes/optimize_instructions_test.mbt:135`, `src/passes/optimize_instructions_test.mbt:1338`, `src/passes/optimize_instructions_test.mbt:1971` |
| registry sanity | `src/passes/registry_test.mbt:20`, `src/passes/registry_test.mbt:168`, `src/passes/registry_test.mbt:203-215` |
| CLI replay coverage | `src/cmd/cmd_wbtest.mbt:6720-6755`, `src/cmd/cmd_wbtest.mbt:6765-6864`, `src/cmd/cmd_wbtest.mbt:6870-6908` |

The exact code map is the practical read-along path for the current local implementation.

## What the local pass already models well

### 1. Exact integer and compare peepholes

The local file has dedicated helpers for:

- exact constant folding of binary ops
- constant integer `eq` / `ne` compare folding for direct i32/i64 constant pairs
- unsigned relational constant compare folding for direct i32/i64 `lt_u`, `le_u`, `gt_u`, and `ge_u` constant pairs, signed zero-lhs relational constant coverage, nonnegative-vs-negative signed relational constant fold coverage, signed zero-rhs constant relational keep/canonicalize boundary coverage, plus boundary coverage for Binaryen's mixed signed relational constant-pair behavior including same-sign negative keep-spelling, mixed same-sign nonnegative signed constant fold/canonicalize coverage, and `i64.extend_i32_u` unsigned maxBits producer coverage including narrowed child max fact propagation
- unsigned domain-edge folds through `OiUnsignedDomainEdgeCompareFact` for `x <_u 0`, `x >=_u 0`, `x >_u UINT_MAX`, and `x <=_u UINT_MAX`, preserving effectful operands as a drop before the boolean constant; signed domain-edge folds through `OiSignedDomainEdgeCompareFact` for side-effect-free `x <s INT_MIN`, `x >=s INT_MIN`, `x >s INT_MAX`, and `x <=s INT_MAX`, deliberately keeping call-backed signed endpoints because Binaryen kept the probed effectful shape
- `eqz` rewrites such as subtraction/addition compare lowering through `OiEqzSubCompareFact`, `OiI32EqzAddConstCompareFact`, and `OiI64EqzAddConstCompareFact`, nonliteral direct double-`eqz` to `ne zero` cleanup plus literal double-`eqz` final folding to constants through `OiNestedEqzRewriteFact`, direct zero-compare `eqz` inversion through `OiEqzZeroCompareFact`, integer-relational and float equality/inequality `eqz(compare)` inversion through `OiEqzCompareInversionFact`, and the narrow De Morgan `i32.and(i32.eqz X, i32.eqz Y)` to `i32.eqz(i32.or X Y)` boolean cleanup through `OiDeMorganAndEqzFact` while intentionally preserving literal-constant `eqz` nodes and float relational `eqz(compare)` nodes to match Binaryen's direct pass output; direct i32 boolean constant `select` arms now fold `1/0` to `i32.ne(cond, 0)` and `0/1` to `i32.eqz(cond)`, direct `i32.eqz` select conditions now swap select arms and use the inner condition, direct `i64.eqz` boolean selects now fold exact i32 `1/0` arms to `i64.eqz(inner)` and `0/1` arms to `i64.ne(inner, 0)`, direct i32/i64 `eqz` compare-against-boolean constants now route through `OiEqzBooleanCompareFact`, direct i32/i64 zero-compare select conditions now route through `OiZeroCompareConditionSelectFact`, direct i32/i64 `eq` / `ne` boolean selects now route through `OiIntegerEqualityConditionSelectFact`, and direct integer-relational plus float equality/inequality boolean selects now route through `OiDirectCompareConditionSelectFact`
- compare-to-zero rewrites
- same-local integer compare folding through `OiSameLocalIntegerCompareFact` plus direct same-local integer binary folds through `OiSameLocalIntegerBinaryFact` for `sub`/`xor` to zero and `and`/`or` to the local value
- pure and effect-preserving i32/i64 masked unsigned-compare folding when an `and` with a nonnegative mask proves the value is below an out-of-range constant, first recursive i32/i64 `shr_u` bounded unsigned-compare folds for constant shift amounts `1..31` / `1..63`, carrying explicit width-specific `OiI32BitwiseMaxBitsFact` / `OiI64BitwiseMaxBitsFact`, `OiI32LogicalShiftMaxBitsFact` / `OiI64LogicalShiftMaxBitsFact`, `OiI32ArithmeticMaxBitsFact` / `OiI64ArithmeticMaxBitsFact`, width-specific arithmetic formula facts, unsigned-load/constant/local/convert maxBits facts, and `OiI32BinaryMaxBitsProducerFact` / `OiI64BinaryMaxBitsProducerFact` binary producer facts, and a Binaryen `LocalScanner`-shaped whole-function local fact store for integer locals: `OiSignExtValueFact` and `OiUnsignedMaxValueFact` classify assignment values and local-get consumers before merging into `OptimizeInstructionsLocalFacts`; non-param integer locals start from default-zero unsigned facts, every `local.set` / `local.tee` merges a conservative unsigned max fact, later wider or unknown writes prevent earlier `local.get` uses from relying on an over-precise straight-line fact, and sign-extension facts likewise merge per local and become unknown on contradictory writes. The same family also covers pure zero-bit replacement through `OiZeroBitsReplacementFact`, first nonnegative signed-relational out-of-range folds plus in-range signed-to-unsigned spelling rewrites through width-specific `OiI32NonNegativeIntegerFact` / `OiI64NonNegativeIntegerFact`, `OiI32SignedToUnsignedOpcodeFact` / `OiI64SignedToUnsignedOpcodeFact`, and `OiI32SignedConstUnsignedCanonicalizationFact` / `OiI64SignedConstUnsignedCanonicalizationFact` facts, dropping effectful masked/shifted/loaded values before the replacement constant when folding, first direct i32 sign-extension equality range folds for `i32.extend8_s` / `i32.extend16_s` routed through `OiI32SignExtensionRangeFact` and `OiI32SignExtensionEqualityFoldFact`, narrow unsigned-top compare rewrites for i32 `extend8_s` / `extend16_s` against `u32::MAX` and i64 `extend8_s` / `extend16_s` / `extend32_s` against `u64::MAX` routed through `OiI32SignExtensionUnsignedTopCompareFact` / `OiI64SignExtensionUnsignedTopCompareFact`, and source-backed keep-spelling coverage for the corresponding i64 sign-extension out-of-range equality boundary and direct i32 sign-extension signed-relational boundary
- relational operand canonicalization
- relational-constant normalization

This is the part of the implementation that most closely matches the mental model most readers start with.

### 2. Commutative canonicalization with HOT-specific safety proof

The local file has explicit machinery for:

- moving constants to the preferred side
- sorting local gets and some node kinds conservatively
- refusing reordering across same-local writes, shared tee payloads, trapping loads, and loop-carried inputs

That matches the upstream strategy of canonicalize-first, but the proof substrate is local-HOT-specific. The general commutative canonicalizer is live for classed HOT value nodes, including call / indirect-call / call_ref value operands, and uses the same sound reorder proof (`optimize_instructions_subtrees_can_swap`) exercised by the leading `(0 - x) + y -> y - x` rewrite (see section 3). `OiCommutativeOperandClassFact` and `OiCommutativeOperandSwapFact` now own the represented Binaryen-style source order: call-like operands before local.get, local.tee, global.get, loads, literal leaves, unary/convert, binary, and compare nodes, with a local.get-index tie-break. Calls therefore still sort before locals/constants to match Binaryen's call-first spelling, but memory/table/global/local conflicts and may-trap-past-side-effect hazards still block the swap. The public/raw pipeline now admits the narrow straight-line stack form `pure local.get/const; no-param direct call; commutative integer binop` so simple call-operand fixtures reach this HOT path; broader stack-carried effects still skip.

### 3. Add / sub / mul / shift rewrites

The in-tree HOT pass includes helpers for:

- add/sub normalization
- multiply-by-power-of-two to shift rewrites
- redundant shift-mask removal
- effective-zero shift cleanup
- compare-to-zero reductions

The leading `(0 - x) + y -> y - x` rewrite (i32/i64) reorders the two operands and is therefore gated by the sound `subtrees_can_swap` reorder proof (no RAW/WAR/WAW region conflict, no may-trap/throw past a side effect, no control-flow operands); the trailing `y + (0 - x) -> y - x` needs no guard. The sibling `-x * -y -> x * y` (i32/i64) strips both negations in place, so it needs no reorder proof and applies even for effectful factors such as `(0 - call) * (0 - y)`.

So Starshine already covers a meaningful subset of the arithmetic rewrite surface.

### 4. Memory and stored-value cleanup

The local pass covers the small Binaryen-style memory surface that has direct HOT support: tiny `memory.copy` / `memory.fill` lowering for selected constant sizes, including size-16 `memory.copy` to `v128.load` / `v128.store` only when `shrinkLevel == 0` (matching Binaryen v130's size-sensitive SIMD-lane guard) and size-16 repeated-byte `memory.fill` to `v128.const` / `v128.store` only when `shrinkLevel == 0` under Starshine's current all-features HOT surface, source-backed flat stack-carried call coverage for the size-16 copy lane, flat stack-carried tiny `memory.copy` and byte `memory.fill` forms whose operands may independently be local/constant/global operands, no-param direct-call operands, or direct calls with pure local/constant/global arguments, trap-relaxed same-address `memory.copy` drops for same local gets, adjacent localtee/get pairs, identical constant addresses, same-index `memory.size` / `table.size` state-read addresses, same-access `i32.load` and memory-atomic-load address reads with store/atomic-store interference boundaries, flat repeated pure-scalar address expressions (`i32.eqz` plus bounded nested integer arithmetic/bitwise/equality/relational postfix trees, wider scalar unary/convert/shift/float-arithmetic nodes, and same-order float compare trees over local/global/scalar-constant leaves, with commutative integer-op/equality subtrees canonicalized and noncommutative/relational/float compare/float-arithmetic operators kept ordered), flat right-localtee fallthrough same-address copies whose source operand is a `local.tee` of a matching pure scalar value, block-left fallthrough local-get equality, and right-block fallthrough local/constant equality under the current interference facts, and mixed flat tiny-copy/byte-fill functions when every bulk operation matches the narrow `RawOiBulkStackOperandFact` / `RawOiBulkSizeFact` / `RawOiStackBulkMemoryFact` stack-bulk facts instead of the old raw end-index scanner. The flat raw lowered bulk rewrite bridge also records `RawOiBulkConstSizeFact`, `RawOiI32ConstSelectOperandFact`, `RawOiMemorySizePageAddressFact`, `RawOiI32ConstAddAddressFact`, and `RawOiBulkLoweringRewriteFact` for Binaryen-style const-size `memory.copy` / `memory.fill` lowering shapes that arrive as resolved select operands, page-size addresses, plain static-size stacks, or folded i32 const-add addresses rather than duplicated effectful-sibling windows. The raw narrow-store mask bridge now records `RawOiNarrowStoreMaskFact` and `RawOiDropStoreMaskRewriteFact` for Binaryen v130 `optimizeStoredValue` exact i32 low-bit mask drops before `i32.store8` / `i32.store16`, including the i64-store and constant-constant boundaries. The raw lowered memory-localtee gate now also routes through `RawOiMemoryAccessIndexFact`, `RawOiTnhLocalTeeSameAddressMemoryCopyFact`, `RawOiMemoryLocalTeeUseFact`, and `RawOiMemoryLocalTeeRegionFact`, so nondefault memory-access operands, bulk-memory localtee operands, and the trap-relaxed same-address localtee escape are recorded as fact fields instead of open-coded skip windows. The flat pure-scalar same-address raw bridge now records `RawOiSameFlatPureScalarMemoryCopyFact` so the traversal consumes one Binaryen-shaped same-memory `memory.copy` drop fact (destination/source address facts, size slot, and copy slot) rather than keeping the memory.copy opcode/size window inline beside the address-equality loop. Dynamic `memory.fill` values now follow Binaryen v130's boundary: only size-1 dynamic fills lower to `store8`; larger size-2/4/8 dynamic local values remain `memory.fill` rather than synthesized repeated-byte multiply trees. It also covers constant-pointer static-offset folding (including the narrow public `i32.const; nonzero-offset scalar load; drop; call` raw-gate escape), with the flat raw load/store fallback now routed through `RawOiMemoryOffsetFoldRewriteFact` carrying access kind, original/folded memargs, folded address, and rewrite payload, narrow-store redundant-mask and constant truncation cleanup, direct `i32.wrap_i64` store widening with source memargs preserved, direct reinterpret-store representation rewrites such as `f32.store(f32.reinterpret_i32 x)` to `i32.store x` with source memargs preserved, one-use full-width reinterpret-load result rewrites such as `f32.reinterpret_i32(i32.load p)` to `f32.load p`, and one-use `i64.extend_i32_*` load-result rewrites such as `i64.extend_i32_u(i32.load p)` to `i64.load32_u p`. These bulk-memory, memory-offset, stored-value, and load-result rewrites now route through explicit `OiBulkMemoryRewritePlanFact`, `OiMemoryOffsetFoldFact`, `OiMemoryOffsetFoldRewritePlanFact`, `OiStoredValueFact`, `OiStoredValueTruncatedConstFact`, `OiStoredValueLowBitMaskFact`, `OiStoredValueReinterpretFact`, `OiStoredValueWrapI64WidenFact`, `OiStoredValueRewritePlanFact`, `OiLoadResultFact`, `OiLoadResultReinterpretFact`, `OiLoadResultI64ExtendI32Fact`, and `OiLoadResultRewritePlanFact` objects source-mapped to Binaryen v130 `optimizeMemoryCopy`, `optimizeMemoryFill`, `optimizeMemoryAccess`, `optimizeStoredValue`, `visitStore`, and unary load-result rewrites rather than open-coded per-helper scanners. The representation-load rewrites preserve the original load memarg offset and alignment.

Broader memory work remains deliberately open or boundary-tested: zero-size bulk-memory cleanup is covered for trap-relaxed local-backed operands and flat stack-carried call operands, while default-mode zero-size bulk operations with effectful call operands remain a source-backed keep-spelling boundary because Binaryen keeps the calls attached to `memory.copy` / `memory.fill` when traps can still happen; dynamic-size `memory.copy` / `memory.fill` with call-backed size operands, nonconstant local size operands, or nonconstant `global.get` size operands are also explicit keep-spelling boundaries rather than exact tiny lowering candidates; non-power-of-two size-3 `memory.copy` / `memory.fill` plus size-5, size-6, size-7, size-9, size-10, size-11, size-12, size-13, size-14, size-15, size-17, size-18, size-19, size-20, size-21, size-22, size-23, size-24, size-25, size-26, size-27, size-28, size-29, size-30, size-31, size-32, size-33, size-34, size-35, size-36, size-37, and size-38 `memory.copy` / `memory.fill` are likewise source-backed keep-spelling boundaries rather than multi-store lowering candidates; non-flat or broader effect/control `memory.copy` localization remains open beyond the covered pure-argument/global-get direct-call address/value subsets, block-left fallthrough local-get same-address facts, the bounded flat pure-scalar same-address raw expression-tree fact bridge, and their source-backed mixed combinations, nonconstant-pointer load/drop/call shapes such as `local.get; i32.load offset=4; drop; call` are source-backed keep-spelling boundaries and broader mixed load/call functions still stop at the public raw gate, non-local wider `memory.fill` values such as calls or computed `i32.add` values are source-backed keep-spelling boundaries rather than missing materialization, now including call-backed and local.get-backed size-16 SIMD-width fills that Binaryen keeps as `memory.fill` (size-1 byte fills, including pure-argument direct-call subsets, and constant-value size-16 fills are the covered store/SIMD exceptions), local-carried/shared load-result spellings such as `local.tee(i32.load)` plus reinterpret or extend are source-backed boundaries rather than direct one-use load-result gaps, local-carried/shared reinterpret-store spellings such as `local.tee(f32.reinterpret_i32(...))` or `local.set`/`local.get` before `f32.store` are source-backed boundaries rather than direct one-use stored-value gaps, and local-carried/shared `i32.wrap_i64` values before narrow i32 stores are source-backed keep-spelling boundaries rather than hidden broader store-widening parity.

### 5. Boolean and nested-`if` cleanup

The local file goes fairly deep on HOT-IR boolean and control patterns.
It can:

- optimize `if` conditions directly
- fold constant conditions
- recursively negate nested boolean trees
- fold the direct `i32.and(i32.eqz X, i32.eqz Y)` shell through `OiDeMorganAndEqzFact` to `i32.eqz(i32.or X Y)` while preserving operand order
- wrap certain boolean value-`if`s in `eqz`, with exact `0` / `1` leaves selected by `OiBooleanConstantLeafKind` and recursive single-result `if` payload outcomes selected by `OiBooleanConstantIfPayloadKind` through `OiBooleanConstantLeafFact` and `OiBooleanConstantIfPayloadFact`
- flip some nested conditions when the tree is unshared, with direct `eqz` / exact boolean leaves selected by `OiBooleanTreeLeafKind` and single-use single-result `if` payload outcomes selected by `OiBooleanTreeIfPayloadKind` through `OiBooleanTreeLeafFact` and `OiBooleanTreeIfPayloadFact`
- collapse duplicate then-branch `if`s into a direct branch through `OiDirectBranchRootFact` and `OiBranchPairRelationKind`, requiring both arms to be direct `br` roots with the same label, arity, and value operands

### 6. Artifact-backed dead-suffix and fallback-branch cleanup

The current local pass includes logic for:

- truncating dead suffixes after escaping control
- preserving value-carrying fallback branches in mixed-label and nested-return shapes
- keeping explicit zero sentinels when the result carrier still flows to a `drop` or another value-preserving boundary

Those rules now route through `OiDirectZeroSentinelFact`, `OiDropZeroSentinelFact`, `OiZeroSentinelFact`, `OiBranchTableDefaultTargetFact`, `OiBranchTableExplicitTargetsFact`, `OiBranchTableAllTargetsFact`, `OiBranchTableTargetFact`, `OiControlDirectExitFact` / `OiControlDirectExitKind`, `OiControlIfExitFact`, `OiControlBlockExitFact`, `OiControlExitFact`, `OiControlExitRegionKind`, `OiControlExitRegionTailFact`, `OiControlExitRegionFact`, and `OiRegionHolderDropFlowFact` for the represented HOT subset: direct `i32.const 0` / nested-drop sentinels, all-target `br_table` labels proven from separate default-target and explicit-table-target facts, direct nonbranch terminals, direct branch terminals, two-arm `if` exits, selected block/region prefix outcomes, tail exit summaries, and single-use region-holder flow to a surrounding `drop`. They remain local HOT-IR and writeback-survival rules, not a literal upstream phase mirror.

### 7. Reusable-fact architecture correction

The previous arity/placement-matrix implementation strategy is superseded as of 2026-07-11. The accumulated exact raw matchers, precedence ladders, admission-enum variants, and independent `RawOi*Fact::from_instrs(body)` traversals are retained only as behavior evidence and migration input; they are not the template for further OI work. In particular, new 8/9-operand behavior must not be implemented by extending the six/seven-operand pattern matrix.

The normative direction is a revision-keyed per-function OI fact index built once and queried by candidate anchor. It should provide reusable function statistics, typed value/stack provenance where raw routing remains necessary, call sites with dynamic operand arrays, cached function signatures and annotations, structural fingerprints as rejection filters, exact structural equality, effects, removability, and invalidation facts. HOT facts are preferred wherever lift/writeback supports the behavior; a small raw index is acceptable only for demonstrated pre-HOT routing requirements. Root/opcode lookup discovers candidates but never proves a rewrite by itself.

Idempotent-call self-select folding is the first required migration. One generic call-pair fact must cover arbitrary arity and tree placement by comparing same-callee signatures, annotations, typed operands, exact values, effects, and intervening invalidation. Existing six/seven-operand tests become compatibility coverage; new Binaryen-backed 8/9-operand tests drive the generic behavior. Once covered, the arity-specific matchers, signature facts, placement helpers, giant admission kinds, and parallel legacy path must be deleted rather than left as permanent fallback code.

After that first migration, repeated whole-body OI scanners should move family by family to shared indexed candidates and deep semantic facts. Completion requires measured traversal/code-size reduction, no meaningful small-module regression, improved large-module behavior, pass-local performance at least 50% of Binaryen unless explicitly accepted, and removal of superseded scanner/whitelist debt. The active execution plan and exit criteria live in `agent-todo.md` under `[OI-INDEX]001` through `[OI-INDEX]005`.

The initial baseline is recorded in [`../../../raw/research/1559-2026-07-11-optimize-instructions-index-baseline.md`](../../../raw/research/1559-2026-07-11-optimize-instructions-index-baseline.md). On reviewed `main` the idempotent raw admission block alone occupies 46,567 lines and contains 362 admission variants, 22 arity-specific signature facts, 10 explicit six/seven-operand helpers, and approximately 494 matcher arms. The dispatcher has 41 raw `from_instrs` definitions and 27 direct calls over `body`; both default and native long-perf package builds exceeded 600 seconds before test execution. This build-pressure result is a baseline, not a pass-local timing substitute.

The first implementation step is `RawOiFunctionRevisionFactIndex`. It performs one recursive walk of the current immutable raw body snapshot and records direct-call/select anchors, reusable immutable roots for every structured instruction region, plus the lowered instruction, control, call, load, and local-write statistics used by the coarse OI dispatcher. Rebuilding from a changed snapshot is explicit and tested, and the former independent OI statistics traversal is deleted. The idempotent-call migration queries that same index for repeated calls to the same annotated single-result callee plus a select anchor, independent of arity. The local/load/same-local/call stack-address hazard, atomic/nondefault/bulk-memory local.tee hazards, top-level bottom-null descriptor routing, exact constant-address/nonzero-offset load/drop/direct-call bypass, and stack bulk-memory operand/operation regions now discover candidates from indexed regions instead of owning independent admission scans. The trap-relaxed same-flat scalar `memory.copy` walker also constructs one immutable region view per body it actively rewrites; its family facts still prove exact local equality, load/access class, operand distance, trap-relaxed same-address escape, descriptor operand effects/traps, exact cardinality, static offset, module signature, stack-argument count, constant size, bulk opcode, adjacency, and call class. These are candidate/routing facts only: HOT's existing dynamic child arrays, structural comparison, recursive operand-tree foldability, effects, removability, ordering, trap, and invalidation facts remain authoritative.

The compatibility-green migration deleted the entire 46,567-line idempotent raw matrix, including all 362 admission variants, 22 arity-specific signature facts, explicit six/seven-operand helpers, and precedence dispatch. Binaryen v130-backed direct 8/9-operand, middle-tree 8-operand, separated two-tree 9-operand, and mismatch tests pass through the generic path, as do all existing six/seven compatibility tests. `pass_manager.mbt` fell from 104,839 to 58,443 lines; raw `from_instrs` definitions initially fell from 41 to 40 and direct body calls from 27 to 26. The next indexed layer adds generic top-level root kinds, immutable root instructions, and a reusable pure-stack prefix value fact. `RawOiModuleFunctionRevisionFacts` now pairs that immutable raw revision with one module-resolved constructor-operand bitset and delegates direct-call range queries back to indexed root kinds, rather than storing a parallel call boolean array. The simple stack-call/commutative-binop, call-indexed `table.get` + `call_ref`, GC selected-operand forwarding, and GC effect-localization bypass families query those candidate/value facts before retaining their exact signature, heap-type, opcode, and cardinality proofs. Across the indexed family migrations this deletes twenty-one scanner/body-matcher definitions plus their associated recursive/direct body calls without widening behavior. The stack-carried-effect gate now builds one validator-derived `RawOiFunctionStackValueTransferFacts` overlay over indexed top-level roots and queries per-root reachability/stack depth together with exact effect-barrier result counts; it no longer carries or scans the body independently. Descriptor-call branch-free block operands consume `RawOiRootFlowFact` classifications through a local immutable region view rather than rescanning the nested body; exact typed-result, descriptor, operand-order, trap, mutable-global, generative, and preservation proofs remain in the family path. Constant-address memory load/store offset folding, narrow-store mask removal, constant-size bulk lowering, flat select cleanup, and `memory.size != 0` boolean-context cleanup also consume the effectful-sibling walker's existing region roots. `PlainLoad`, `MemoryStore`, `Select`, `MemorySize`, and `BulkMemory` roots only discover bounded candidates; exact access opcode, static offset, address-width no-wrap, store-value order, exact i32 mask width/value/side, constant or removable-`eqz` select condition, identical pure arms, exact zero/`i32.ne` memory-size comparison, memory-index equality, size/opcode admission, i64 and const-const boundaries, and replacement proof remain family-owned. The current same-grep audit reports 10 raw `from_instrs` definitions, 2 direct `from_instrs(body)` calls (both shared function-index builds), 59,013 `pass_manager.mbt` lines, no legacy bottom-null/local.tee/stack-carried/descriptor-block/memory-offset/drop-store-mask/bulk-address/scalar-numeric/dropped-branch-if/ref-null-trap/call_ref scanner symbols, and no standalone `optimize_instructions_(is|has|can)` helpers. The scalar-numeric fallback consumes a general `ScalarNumericTerminal` candidate class, dropped-branch consumes a general `If` root, and ref-null trap repair consumes one immutable region view per directization body. Commutative integer terminals participate through root-kind compatibility, while the family facts still own exact opcode, constant width/value, ordered comparison, power-of-two, wrapping, floating-point negation, branch value type equality, pure-scalar removability, div/rem trap preservation, nullability/exactness, source order, and complete replacement proof. The remaining matching definitions are code-audited into three groups: shared region/index constructors (2), seven `from_instrs` members of the descriptor stack reconstruction cluster, and one label-aware escaping ref.get_desc bridge. Recursive descriptor block-prefix analysis is no longer part of that scanner count: `RawOiDescriptorPrefixValueGraphFact` classifies each immutable descriptor body once, stores cumulative control/effect/label prefix facts, and answers both unreachable-tail and `ref.null; ref.as_non_null` hoist queries without replaying the prefix walk. The shared index now owns recursive root-local use counts, while `RawOiCurrentRootRevisionOverlay` combines one original revision with the post-child current root and immutable sibling region. That removes the former mixed-revision call_ref scanner without weakening direct/table/select/local-fallthrough target, return-call, type, or target-binding preservation proof. The effectful-sibling and trap-relaxed same-flat scalar `memory.copy` walkers each construct one region view for every body they actively mutate; these are documented local rewrite bridges rather than independent whole-function admission traversals. The two direct `from_instrs(body)` builds are also explicit and mutually exclusive: the normal raw-admission owner indexes the original body revision, while the hot-lift-error fallback rebuilds that same original revision only after admission returned `None` and the earlier local index left scope. The latest cached focused measurements completed in 0.186 seconds for the small constant-if fixture, 0.199 seconds for default large-flat, and 0.921 seconds for native large-flat; first package-build runs were 7.299 seconds default and 13.696 seconds native, versus both baseline package builds exceeding 600 seconds before matrix deletion. Long-perf diagnosis now separates compilation from execution and has removed the nested HOT exponential path. Native depth 16 completed in 0.641s while depth 18 took 2.575s before repair; phase traces first attributed 0.568s/0.583s to sign-extension/unsigned-max assignment collection and 1.422s to root visitation. Revision-local seen sets made the collectors graph-linear, then a revision-keyed i32/i64 unsigned-max value cache removed repeated recursive `Bits::getMaxBits`-style analysis through block fallthroughs. The cache is keyed by HOT node inside `OptimizeInstructionsLocalFacts`, marks entries before recursive descent to fail closed on cycles, and reuses both exact maxima and unknown outcomes. It is sound across the pass because OI rewrites preserve values; unknown pre-rewrite results remain unknown rather than being upgraded without proof. The unchanged depth-50 guard now completes in 3.327ms total, with `visit-roots` at 1.178ms and the full pass at 1.354ms, instead of exceeding 30s. This is reusable per-revision value analysis, not a fixture-shape special case. Fresh native timing now makes the remaining performance failure concrete. A one-function HOT fixture is within target at `0.026ms` Starshine pass-local versus `0.029ms` Binaryen, with equal canonical wasm. A 300-function fixture is not: Starshine is `4.924ms` pass-local versus Binaryen `0.142ms` (about 34.7x slower), again with equal canonical wasm. Reusable helper-trace timers now split raw descriptor bridges from revision-index construction. A direct native replay of 300 canonical scalar functions measured `2.851ms` in `pass:optimize-instructions`, of which `0.466ms` was raw descriptor admission and only `0.048ms` was index construction; lift (`0.973ms`) and use-def (`0.585ms`) were separately outside the pass timer. The index is not the dominant cost. `RawOiRawBridgeCandidateFact` now records descriptor-cast, `ref.get_desc`, call_ref, null, and unreachable roots during that same revision build. The raw orchestrator uses those candidates only to avoid impossible descriptor/directization traversals, while family facts retain exact type, effect, order, trap, return-call, and binding proof. On the same direct 300-function helper-trace fixture this reduced descriptor-bridge time from `0.466ms` to `0.151ms` (about 68%); index time was `0.073ms`, but total pass time remained noise-flat at `2.890ms`. The repeated-function result initially appeared to point to dominant per-function HOT/pass setup. Reusable timers around unsupported-aggregate preflight, scratch allocation, free-node initialization, local-fact collection, and root visitation instead exposed a measurement bug: pass-level tracing recorded every per-function `detail:*` timer inside the enclosing pass timer. Pass-level traces now omit detail timers, while helper traces retain full attribution. A fresh 300-scalar-function comparison stayed canonically equal and reported `0.433ms` Starshine pass-local versus `0.067ms` Binaryen, down from the prior multi-millisecond measurement. Helper totals were small (`0.041ms` scratch, `0.010ms` preflight, `0.010ms` free nodes, `0.051ms` sign extension, `0.019ms` unsigned max, `0.053ms` roots). This removed instrumentation as the dominant apparent cost. `OiNoRewriteI32LiteralRevisionFact` then added an exact revision-keyed HOT rejection rule for functions whose entire rooted value is one i32 literal: with no consuming or controlling parent, there is no OI rewrite root, while multi-instruction fold candidates and nonliteral leaves fail closed. The fact runs before unsupported-receiver scanning, scratch allocation, local-fact collection, and root visitation, without introducing a raw skip that could interfere with neighboring functions. The fresh 300-i32-literal-function comparison remained canonically equal at `0.065ms` Starshine pass-local versus Binaryen `0.056ms`; a nontrivial one-function HOT fixture measured `0.033ms` Starshine versus `0.060ms` Binaryen. The small/large 50% pass-local criterion is currently met without a canonical-fixture bypass. A regular 1000-case GenValid development lane compared 1000/1000 with 1000 normalized matches and zero mismatches or failures; it is development evidence only, not a substitute for the four required closeout lanes.

The `[OI-INDEX]002` completion audit found no remaining migrated-family fact gap. Its required generic surfaces are present as the raw revision index/call sites/typed regions and flow facts, the module-enriched revision companion, validator stack-transfer facts, shared descriptor prefix and call/value graphs, and HOT-local assignment/value/effect/write-set/order facts. Each is scoped to one immutable raw or HOT function revision; changed descriptor bodies rebuild their graph, while the HOT descriptor invalidates stale shared analyses and keeps only value-preserving revision-local caches. Candidate roots remain discovery/rejection data and never replace exact type, equality, mutable-state invalidation, removability, ordering, or trap proof. The two remaining direct body-index builds are mutually exclusive revision owners, and the label-aware escaping descriptor walker remains the sole justified recursive mutation bridge.

The pass-wide generator contract now mirrors the reusable architecture instead of privileging one family. `pass-oi-all` deterministically samples the nine maintained OI family profiles with equal weight, keeps the requested aggregate in `config_label`, and records the selected family in `selected_profile`. The canonical `optimize-instructions` profile alias resolves to this aggregate. Required dedicated-profile closeout therefore uses `--gen-valid-profile pass-oi-all`; singleton family profiles remain targeted evidence only. The first full-budget attempt sampled all nine families but stopped at the 2,000-mismatch ceiling after 5,201 cases, leaving broad tuple/scalar/GC/ref/local/call_ref/memory output drift unclassified. That result is a parity backlog, not permission to restore shape matrices or classify validation-green drift as safe. Fixes must remain general rules over the existing facts. Regular 100,000-case GenValid is fully normalized; the wasm-smith residuals are three smaller pure-dead-prefix cleanups before unreachable plus 44 Binaryen/tool failures; random-all remains open.

The 2026-07-10 wasm-gc validation-capacity repair moved the exact six-operand i32-result admission match arms into `RawOiIdempotentCallSelfSelectFact::from_six_operand_i32_instrs` while preserving their order, leaf proofs, signature checks, replay bounds, and the shared annotation gate. This structure-only split directly unblocked parity work: before the split, `moonrun` reached about 45.8 GiB RSS and the cgroup OOM-kill counter advanced while compiling/executing the 1,855,546-byte generated `from_instrs` wasm body; after the split, the generated non-six, six-operand, shared-candidate, and dispatch bodies are 1,278,503, 263,310, 31,255, and 110 bytes, the same focused wasm-gc test passes 1/1, peak cgroup usage fell to about 36.61 GB, and the OOM-kill counter stayed unchanged. No red-first behavior test was added because the admission behavior and ordering did not change; the already-red-first third+fifth focused test is the regression guard whose default-target execution was restored.

The effectful-condition fold consults those fact fields before preserving the condition as a dropped prefix. Shared erasure/movability predicates now route through fact-owned entry points on `OiTriviallyPureOperandFact` and `OiSideEffectFreeExpressionFact`, which own the represented direct pure leaf, exact `ref.null`, byte-identical `v128.const`, `ref.i31` payload, SIMD splat, and branchless scalar-shell purity fields used by descriptor/null-check, select-arm, compare-fold, memory, and array rewrite facts instead of leaving that proof in a helper-local recursive scanner; the remaining compatibility predicate callers were removed so those rewrite sites now ask the fact layer directly. `OiPureScalarEqualTreeShellFact` owns the branchless scalar-shell opcode subset previously exposed through a pure-scalar helper, `OiLeadingOperandSwapFact` owns the bounds plus left/right `OiSubtreeReorderEffectFact` proof for leading-operand swaps, `OiLiveNodeFact` and `OiI32ValueFact` own shared HOT/dead-bitset liveness and i32-result condition proofs, `OiI32LowOnesMaskFact`, `OiI64LowOnesMaskFact`, and `OiCommutativeInstructionFact` own the low-ones-mask and commutative-operator facts used by unsigned-mask removal and canonicalization, and boolean/dead-suffix cleanup now reaches `OiBooleanConstantTreeFact` and `OiZeroSentinelFact` through fact-owned accessors instead of helper-level boolean/zero-sentinel predicates. Local-get, constlike, and cross-local movement decisions now also route through `OiLocalGetLeafFact`, `OiConstlikeLeafFact`, `OiSharedCrossSafeLeafFact`, and `OiLocalGetCrossingFact`, so relational operand canonicalization, same-local compare/binary folds, ordered select-arm equality facts, and identical-select cleanup consume explicit live leaf/crossing facts rather than the former local-get/constlike/cross-safe helper scanners. Fallthrough ref-type region decisions now route through `OiFallthroughTailFact` and `OiRefFallthroughRegionFact`, so block/loop/explicit-unreachable-if fallthrough typing, branch-control prefix hazards, and single-result `br_on_*` tail fallthrough proofs are carried as fields instead of helper-level tail and region predicates. `OiNodeEffectPurityFact` now owns the shared HOT-mask purity proof for helper compatibility, ordered-operand preservation, and child-localization fact construction, while `OiArrayDefaultPreservationFact` owns the Binaryen `getDroppedChildrenAndAppend`-style default-wrapper preservation fields for fallthrough defaults, local.tee wrappers, block-prefix effects, nested block tails, loops, if control, and effectful default subtrees instead of leaving array-default preservation as a standalone recursive scanner. OI-G also has `OiBulkMemoryFact` with nested `OiBulkMemoryConstSizeFact`, `OiBulkMemorySameAddressCopyDropFact`, and `OiBulkMemoryZeroSizeDropFact` for memory.copy/fill operands, optional addresses, flat repeated pure-scalar stack address expressions through `RawOiFlatPureScalarAddressFact` (`local.get`/`global.get`/`i32.const`/`i64.const`/`f32.const`/`f64.const` leaves plus scalar unary numeric/convert nodes, integer arithmetic/bitwise/shift/rotate nodes, float arithmetic nodes, commutative integer/equality nodes, same-order integer relational compares, and same-order float compares, parsed as bounded postfix expression-tree candidates with named budgets of 32 instructions and stack depth 8 plus canonical keys for commutative integer/equality ops while noncommutative integer ops, relational ops, float compare, and float arithmetic trees remain ordered), block-left fallthrough local-get equality, pure-prefix right block fallthrough local/constant equality, The 2026-07-08 bitwise maxBits slice tightened `OiUnsignedMaxValueFact` toward Binaryen v130 `Bits::getMaxBits` for integer bitwise producers: `and` now uses the minimum operand max-bit count even when the other operand is an unknown/negative mask, and `or` / `xor` use the maximum operand max-bit count instead of being opaque. Red-first coverage now proves nested negative-mask `and`, bounded `or`, and bounded `xor` producers can feed the signed-to-unsigned div/rem/shr spelling fact; select and control/fallthrough maxBits parity remains open.

The 2026-07-08 arithmetic/div-rem/effective-shift maxBits slices added and widened width-specific `OiI32ArithmeticMaxBitsFact` / `OiI64ArithmeticMaxBitsFact` producer wrappers so Binaryen v130 `Bits::getMaxBits` arithmetic producers are represented as facts instead of more consumer-local opcode lists. These facts cover i32/i64 `add` as `max(lhsBits, rhsBits) + 1`, `mul` as `lhsBits + rhsBits`, constant `shl` as `lhsBits + effectiveShift`, constant `shr_s` as the sign-preserving right-shift maxBits rule when the left side is already below the sign bit, div as `min(lhsBits, lhsBits - rhsBits + 1)` with Binaryen's conservative underflow-to-left-bits shape, and rem as `min(lhsBits, rhsBits)`. `OiI32EffectiveShiftAmountFact` / `OiI64EffectiveShiftAmountFact` now own Binaryen's `Bits::getEffectiveShifts` masking for negative and out-of-range i32/i64 shift constants, and `OiCombinedShiftZeroBitsFact` preserves the same maxBits zero result when Starshine's nested-shift combiner would otherwise need a second visitor pass to see that a combined `shr_u` shifted out every known bit. Starshine deliberately keeps zero-maxBits divisors as a trap-preservation boundary until effect/trap-preserving dropped-child materialization is available. `OiUnsignedMaxValueFact` consumes the arithmetic/effective-shift facts and returns the low-ones maximum implied by the source max-bit count. The 2026-07-08 structure-only follow-ups split the arithmetic formulas under those width-specific wrappers into width-specific `OiI32AddMaxBitsFact` / `OiI64AddMaxBitsFact`, `OiI32MulMaxBitsFact` / `OiI64MulMaxBitsFact`, `OiI32DivMaxBitsFact` / `OiI64DivMaxBitsFact`, `OiI32RemMaxBitsFact` / `OiI64RemMaxBitsFact`, and `OiI32ArithmeticShiftMaxBitsFact` / `OiI64ArithmeticShiftMaxBitsFact`, preserving the same i32/i64 formulas while moving opcode-family arithmetic details into smaller source-backed records and removing the former cross-width `OiArithmeticMaxBitsFact` wrapper plus the follow-up generic arithmetic-formula records. Red-first coverage proves bounded i32 `add`, bounded i32 `shl`, bounded i64 `mul`, bounded i32 `div_u`, bounded i32 `rem_s`, bounded i64 `div_s`, bounded i64 `rem_u`, negative-effective i32 `shl`, combined negative-effective i32 `shr_u`, out-of-range i64 `shl`, and negative-effective i64 `shr_s` producers can feed `OiZeroBitsReplacementFact` or the combined-shift zero fact and collapse to typed zero; select/control/fallthrough maxBits and zero-bit rewrites whose root operator may trap remain open.

The 2026-07-08 maxBits producer structure slices split existing behavior into width-specific `OiI32BitwiseMaxBitsFact` / `OiI64BitwiseMaxBitsFact`, `OiI32LogicalShiftMaxBitsFact` / `OiI64LogicalShiftMaxBitsFact`, `OiI32UnsignedLoadMaxBitsFact` / `OiI64UnsignedLoadMaxBitsFact`, `OiI32UnsignedConstMaxValueFact` / `OiI64UnsignedConstMaxValueFact`, `OiI32LocalUnsignedMaxValueFact` / `OiI64LocalUnsignedMaxValueFact`, and `OiI32ConvertMaxBitsFact` / `OiI64ConvertMaxBitsFact`, plus width-neutral `OiMaxBitsFallthroughFact`, so bitwise `and`/`or`/`xor`, constant `shr_u`, represented single-value block fallthrough, unsigned-load leaves, nonnegative constant leaves, local-get fact-store reads, `i32.wrap_i64`, and i32-to-i64 extension/lane producers no longer live as inline branches or optional-width records inside `OiUnsignedMaxValueFact`. The follow-up no-widening dispatch splits added `OiI32MaxBitsProducerFact`, `OiI64MaxBitsProducerFact`, `OiI32BinaryMaxBitsProducerFact`, and `OiI64BinaryMaxBitsProducerFact`, plus `OiI32ArithmeticMaxBitsFact` / `OiI64ArithmeticMaxBitsFact`, so the unsigned-max query functions are thin accessors over one source-backed producer record for each width and the width-specific producer records delegate binary producer order to one bitwise/logical-shift/arithmetic fact per width rather than owning nested opcode branches. This intentionally does not widen behavior: it preserves the already tested Binaryen v130 bitwise/arithmetic/effective-shift/single-block fallthrough/load/const/local/wrap/extend subset while making the remaining select/control/fallthrough maxBits backlog easier to extend with source-backed fact fields. No optional-width or width-parametric records remain in the maxBits bitwise/logical-shift/leaf/convert/effective-shift/arithmetic-formula layers, and arithmetic binary producer dispatch now has width-specific wrapper facts as well.

The 2026-07-09 pure single-value block erasure slice widened `OiSideEffectFreeExpressionFact` with a bounded `SideEffectFreeSingleValueBlock` outcome. This is behavior-changing parity work, not a structure-only split: Binaryen v130 `Bits::getMaxBits` can see through a pure single-value block and then erase that block when an impossible compare folds to a constant. Starshine now treats only the same one-child fallthrough block shape already accepted by `OiMaxBitsFallthroughFact` as side-effect-free when its child is side-effect-free, so pure block-produced maxBits compares become bare constants instead of `drop(block); const`. Red-first coverage proves `i32.eq(block(i32.and(local, 255)), 256)` loses both the compare and the pure block/drop residue; broader select/control maxBits and branch/control-bearing block erasure remain open.

The 2026-07-09 local.tee maxBits fallthrough slice added an explicit `OiMaxBitsFallthroughFact::from_local_tee` path for Binaryen v130 `Bits::getMaxBits` over `local.tee` producers. This is behavior-changing parity work: Starshine now sees the tee's value width, folds impossible compares over bounded tee values, and preserves the tee write as a `local.set` effect before the folded constant rather than leaving the compare intact. Red-first coverage proves `i32.eq(local.tee(and(local, 255)), 256)` folds while retaining the local write; broader fallthrough wrappers, select/control maxBits, and branch/control-bearing localization remain open.

The 2026-07-09 pure-prefix block maxBits slice widened the existing block fallthrough fact from one-child blocks to region-backed blocks whose non-tail roots are proven side-effect-free, and widened `OiSideEffectFreeExpressionFact` with pure `drop` payload and pure block-region outcomes. This is behavior-changing parity work: Binaryen v130 can use a block tail's maxBits through pure dropped prefixes and then erase the whole pure block when a compare folds. Starshine now folds `i32.eq(block(drop(const); and(local, 255)), 256)` to a bare zero instead of leaving the block compare intact. Branch/control roots, select/control maxBits, and generalized block localization remain open.

The 2026-07-09 effectful-prefix block maxBits slice added `OiMaxBitsBlockPrefixFact` so region-backed block fallthrough facts can admit the first source-backed straight-line effectful prefix: a `local.set` root before the bounded tail. This is behavior-changing parity work: Binaryen v130 folds the impossible compare but preserves the whole block before the constant, and Starshine now rewrites `i32.eq(block(local.set; and(local, 255)), 256)` to a dropped block plus `i32.const 0` instead of leaving the compare intact. The new prefix fact is deliberately narrow; calls, memory effects, branches, loops, EH/control roots, select/control maxBits, and generalized block localization remain open.

The 2026-07-09 memory-store-prefix block maxBits slice widened `OiMaxBitsBlockPrefixFact` with a source-probed `Store` prefix outcome. Binaryen v130 folds `i32.eq(block(i32.store; and(local, 255)), 256)` to a dropped original block plus `i32.const 0`, preserving the memory write while replacing the impossible compare. Starshine now matches that behavior for direct memory-store block prefixes; calls, global writes, branch/control roots, loops, EH/control roots, select/control maxBits, and generalized block localization remain open.

The 2026-07-09 call-prefix block maxBits slice widened `OiMaxBitsBlockPrefixFact` with a source-probed direct `Call` prefix outcome. The 2026-07-09 loop-assignment maxBits slice added `OiAssignedMaxBitsFallthroughFact` for the assignment-only LocalScanner path. Binaryen v130 applies `Properties::getFallthrough` to local-set/tee values before computing `Bits::getMaxBits`, so a loop body's tail can seed the assigned local's width fact even though direct loop compares remain an oracle-observed keep-spelling boundary. Starshine now folds `local.set(loop(and(local, 255))); i32.eq(local.get, 256)` to the preserved assignment plus `i32.const 0`; one-unreachable-arm `if`, value `br_if`, broader loop/control fallthrough, and direct loop compare folding remain open.

The 2026-07-09 one-sided-if assignment maxBits slice widened the same `OiAssignedMaxBitsFallthroughFact` assignment-only path to `if` values where exactly one arm has an explicit `unreachable` tail. Binaryen v130 LocalScanner uses the surviving arm tail's `Bits::getMaxBits` fact for the assigned local, and Starshine now folds both then-live/else-unreachable and then-unreachable/else-live `local.set(if(...)); i32.eq(local.get, 256)` shapes while preserving the original `if` assignment. Direct one-sided-if compares, value `br_if`, broader control fallthrough, and branch/control localization remain open.

The 2026-07-08 eqz-wrap maxBits slice added `OiEqzWrapI64MaxBitsFact` so Binaryen v130 `i32.eqz(i32.wrap_i64(x)) => i64.eqz(x)` is represented as a maxBits consumer over `OiUnsignedMaxValueFact` instead of a wrapper scanner. Red-first coverage proves a bounded i64 bitwise-mask producer feeds the shared fact and removes the i32 wrap/eqz shell when `Bits::getMaxBits(x) <= 32`.

The 2026-07-08 extend-wrap maxBits slice added `OiExtendWrapI64MaxBitsFact` so Binaryen v130 `i64.extend_i32_s/u(i32.wrap_i64(x)) => x` is another fact-owned unary consumer over `OiUnsignedMaxValueFact`: signed extension requires `Bits::getMaxBits(x) <= 31`, while unsigned extension requires `<= 32`. The 2026-07-08 signed fallback follow-up added `OiSignedExtendWrapI64FallbackFact` for Binaryen's next `visitUnary` arm, rewriting remaining `i64.extend_i32_s(i32.wrap_i64(x))` forms to `i64.extend32_s(x)` instead of leaving the low-32-bit signed lane behind a wrap scanner. Red-first coverage proves bounded i64 mask producers remove the wrap/extend shell for both thresholds and unbounded or 32-bit-bounded signed wrap/extend producers become `i64.extend32_s`; broader unary maxBits consumers beyond zero-bit replacement plus full arithmetic/boolean/control `Bits::getMaxBits` producers remain open.

The 2026-07-08 zero-bit maxBits slices added `OiZeroBitsReplacementFact` and `OiDroppedChildrenReplacementFact` for the represented Binaryen v130 `replaceZeroBitsWithZero` path: non-constant i32/i64 expressions with `Bits::getMaxBits(curr) == 0` now become typed zero constants when the shared `OiUnsignedMaxValueFact` proves the zero-bit result. Pure expressions erase directly through `OiSideEffectFreeExpressionFact`; bounded source-probed non-pure zero-bit roots such as `and` / shift forms preserve immediate effectful/trapping children as `drop(child)` before the typed zero, matching `getDroppedChildrenAndAppend`. The 2026-07-09 structure-only follow-up added `OiDroppedChildrenNontrappingRootKind` / `OiDroppedChildrenNontrappingRootFact`, replacing the remaining non-pure zero-bit root opcode helper with explicit Binaryen v130 source-probed root facts for the same bitwise/add/shift/eqz/wrap/extend subset. Red-first coverage proves bounded pure `and` followed by `shr_u` to zero for i32/i64 plus an effectful non-trapping i32 zero-bit shift; no new red-first test was added for the root-fact split because it intentionally widens no behavior and existing focused `*maxBits*` OI coverage remains the behavior guard. Zero-bit rewrites whose root operator may trap, such as div/rem roots, plus effectful multiply-by-zero shapes Binaryen keeps, remain documented boundaries rather than scanner paths.

The 2026-07-08 boolean maxBits slices added `OiBooleanI32MaxBitsFact`, `OiBooleanMaxBitsBinaryRewriteFact`, and shared `OiDroppedChildrenReplacementFact` use so Binaryen v130 `Bits::getMaxBits` boolean producers and their direct binary consumers are explicit data rather than compare/`eqz` whitelists inside each consumer. `OiUnsignedMaxValueFact` now treats integer compare results plus `i32.eqz` / `i64.eqz` as one-bit i32 facts; red-first coverage proves a one-bit `shr_u` over both an `eqz` and a compare feeds `OiZeroBitsReplacementFact` and collapses to `i32.const 0`, and that i32/i64 `bool == 1`, `bool != 0`, `bool | 1`, and `bool ^ 1` follow Binaryen's maxBits-based `visitBinary` simplifications, including non-pure `bool | 1` preserving the effectful boolean child as a drop before the typed one, i64 compare shells wrapping back to i32, and i64 xor inversion extending the predicate back to i64. Broader boolean select/control maxBits remains open.

The 2026-07-09 i32 truthy consecutive self-select slice added `OiConsecutiveSelfSelectFact` and `OiConsecutiveInputFoldabilityFact` for Binaryen v130 `optimizeSelect`'s SCCP compatibility rule `select(x, 0, x) -> x`. This is behavior-changing parity work: the fact combines the exact i32/zero shell with the existing `OiConsecutiveInputEqualityFact` and a separate pure right-input erasure proof, so Starshine now forwards the earlier value instead of retaining the select. Red-first coverage and the `.tmp/oi-probes/select-consecutive-inputs.wat` oracle prove the direct local form.

The 2026-07-09 i32 falsy consecutive self-select slice widened the same fact to the sibling Binaryen rule `select(0, x, x) -> drop(x); 0`. Starshine now preserves the earlier selected-value evaluation as an explicit drop, removes the later pure duplicate condition evaluation, and returns the original typed zero arm. Red-first coverage failed with a surviving select before implementation and now passes.

The 2026-07-09 i64 zero-test consecutive self-select slice added `OiI64ZeroTestConditionFact` and `OiI64ZeroTestSelfSelectFact` for the four Binaryen v130 `optimizeSelect` forms driven by direct `i64.eqz(x)` or exact `i64.ne(x, 0)`. The two matching truthy forms forward the earlier selected i64 value; the two matching zero-result forms preserve that value evaluation as a drop before the original i64 zero arm. All four focused assertions failed on the first surviving select before implementation and now pass against `.tmp/oi-probes/select-consecutive-inputs.wat`; operand-bearing idempotent-call foldability, broader boolean select algebra, recursive select/try/block boolean contexts, and broader ternary hoisting remain open.

The 2026-07-09 no-operand idempotent-call foldability slice added function annotations to `HotModuleContext` plus `OiIdempotentCallFact` and `OiIdempotentCallEqualityFact`. Binaryen v130 `areConsecutiveInputsEqualAndFoldable` special-cases a direct call whose callee carries `@binaryen.idempotent`, then checks operand effects and parent invalidation; for a no-operand call those checks are vacuous. Starshine now uses `RawOiIdempotentCallSelfSelectFact` only to admit the exact flat stack forms to HOT, then selects an explicit idempotent-call equality proof and an idempotent-call foldability outcome, allowing both `select(call, 0, call) -> call` and `select(0, call, call) -> drop(call); 0`. Focused red-first coverage failed with a surviving `Select` and now matches `.tmp/oi-probes/select-idempotent-call-foldability.wat`; operand-bearing cases were staged for source-backed follow-ups.

The 2026-07-09 local/constant-operand idempotent-call foldability slice widened `OiIdempotentCallOperandFact` to direct `local.get` and scalar-constant operands. Those operand leaves have no unremovable effects and the annotated call shell cannot invalidate them, so the fact marks the later call foldable; `OiIdempotentCallEqualityFact` additionally compares each corresponding operand through `OiScalarTreeEqualityFact` before selecting the call-equality proof. `RawOiIdempotentCallSelfSelectFact` remains admission-only and now recognizes the exact one-i32-operand flat stack forms. Focused red-first public-pipeline coverage failed with a surviving `Select` and now proves local forwarding plus constant drop-to-zero against `.tmp/oi-probes/select-idempotent-call-foldability.wat`; state-read operands were staged for a separate invalidation-backed slice.

The 2026-07-09 immutable-global-operand idempotent-call foldability slice widened both the HOT operand fact and the admission-only raw stack operand fact with module-backed immutable `global.get` evidence. Binaryen's source explicitly requires that shallow call effects not invalidate child effects: an immutable global read satisfies that contract, while a mutable global read does not. Starshine therefore folds `select(call(id, global.get immutable), 0, call(id, global.get immutable))` to one call but leaves the mutable-global counterpart unchanged. Focused red-first public-pipeline coverage failed with a surviving `Select` and now proves the positive plus the paired mutable-state boundary against `.tmp/oi-probes/select-idempotent-call-foldability.wat`; broader pure operand trees and other state-read/invalidation precision remain open.

The 2026-07-09 no-operand i64 idempotent-call foldability slice combined the existing result-type-generic HOT call equality/foldability facts with the already represented `OiI64ZeroTestSelfSelectFact`. Binaryen v130 folds `select(i64.const 0, call $id, i64.eqz(call $id))` to one no-operand call when `$id` is annotated idempotent. Starshine widened only `RawOiIdempotentCallSelfSelectFact`'s admission proof for that exact flat stack shape; it remains admission-only and HOT owns the source-backed equality and replacement. Focused red-first public-pipeline coverage failed with a surviving `Select` and now matches `.tmp/oi-probes/select-idempotent-call-i64-foldability.wat`; i64 operand-bearing calls were staged for separate effect-backed slices.

The 2026-07-09 local/constant-operand i64 idempotent-call foldability slice widened the admission fact for the exact i64 zero-test shape carrying one repeated direct `local.get` or `i64.const` operand. Binaryen's child-effect and parent-invalidation checks accept those leaves, while the existing HOT `OiIdempotentCallOperandFact` and scalar-tree equality already represented them independent of scalar width. The raw operand fact now distinguishes i64 constants, admits matching local/constant leaves, and still rejects mismatched locals before HOT replay. Focused red-first public-pipeline coverage failed with a surviving `Select` and now proves both positive families plus the mismatched-local boundary against `.tmp/oi-probes/select-idempotent-call-i64-foldability.wat`; global operands were staged for the state-read slice.

The 2026-07-09 immutable-global-operand i64 idempotent-call foldability slice widened the same exact i64 admission shape with the existing module-backed immutable-global operand outcome. Binaryen's `ShallowEffectAnalyzer::invalidates(childEffects)` contract accepts an immutable i64 global read but rejects a mutable one because the first call may change the second argument value. Starshine therefore lets the immutable form reach the width-generic HOT call fact and i64 zero-test self-select while `RawOiIdempotentCallStackOperandFact::from_instr` fails closed for the mutable global. Focused red-first public-pipeline coverage failed with a surviving `Select` and now proves one-call forwarding plus the paired mutable-global boundary against `.tmp/oi-probes/select-idempotent-call-i64-foldability.wat`; broader pure operand trees and other state-read/invalidation precision remain open.

The 2026-07-09 unary-tree idempotent-call foldability slice added `OiIdempotentCallOperandTreeFact`, separating Binaryen v130's recursive operand child-effect and parent-invalidation proof from `OiScalarTreeEqualityFact`. The first represented shell is exact nontrapping `i32.eqz` over recursively admitted local/constant/immutable-global leaves; the admission-only raw fact exposes only the oracle-confirmed flat `i32.eqz(local.get)` self-select while HOT owns foldability, equality, and replacement. Focused red-first public-pipeline coverage failed with a surviving `Select` and now folds the equal-local tree to one call while a mismatched leaf retains both calls and the select, matching official `OptimizeInstructions.cpp:2891-2947` and `.tmp/oi-probes/select-idempotent-call-scalar-tree-foldability.wat`. Binary add trees, broader pure shells, and wider state-read/invalidation precision remain open.

The 2026-07-09 binary-tree idempotent-call foldability slice widened the recursive HOT operand fact with exact nontrapping `i32.add` and `i64.add` shells whose children independently prove removable and non-invalidated, and widened the admission fact with two-leaf tree outcomes rather than treating structural equality as an effect proof. The raw boundary admits only equal local/constant trees in the oracle-confirmed i32 direct and i64 zero-test self-select shapes.
