This is structure-only/no-widening: identical-select-arm cleanup still recognizes only equal `v128.const` leaves or same-instruction v128 splats over the same direct `local.get` child, with v128 splat proof still delegated to `OiUnaryLocalEqualityFact`. No red-first test was added because behavior intentionally did not change; existing focused `*select*` OI coverage remains the behavior guard. Remaining OI-F equality/select breadth still includes ref.i31 payload, nontrapping-reorderable, identical-pure, and broader select-condition compare facts.

The 2026-07-09 ordered binary local-constant equality structure slice added `OiOrderedBinaryLocalConstEqualityKind` under `OiOrderedBinaryLocalConstEqualityFact`, replacing the four parallel i32/i64/f32/f64 local-constant match booleans with one selected Binaryen v130 `ExpressionAnalyzer::equal` proof kind. This intentionally widens no behavior: represented identical-select-arm and effectful-condition cleanup still accepts only same-instruction ordered local+constant scalar shells whose left operands are the same `local.get` and whose right operands are the same typed constant. Existing focused `*select*` coverage remains the guard while broader OI-F select-condition and equality breadth beyond represented direct shells stays source-evidence gated.

The 2026-07-07 `ref.eq` TNH operand `skipCast` slice added `OiRefEqSkipCastFact` so Binaryen v130 `visitRefEq` nullable-eq required-type cast removal under `--traps-never-happen` is represented as a fact-driven operand rewrite after the original impossible-heap proof. Focused red-first coverage now proves default mode preserves a potentially trapping `(ref.cast (ref null i31) (local.get eqref))` operand while TNH erases the cast and leaves `ref.eq` comparing the original nullable-eq operand.

The 2026-07-07 ordinary `ref.cast` child-cast slice added `OiRefCastChildCastFact` so Binaryen v130 `visitRefCast` child `RefCast` removal after known-result folds is represented as a plan fact: if the parent ref type is a subtype of the child ref type, the parent rewires directly to the child cast's operand. Focused red-first coverage now proves a nested nullable same-type `ref.cast` pair keeps one trap-preserving cast instead of two. The 2026-07-08 child subtype structure follow-up added `OiRefCastChildSubtypeFact` / `OiRefCastChildSubtypeKind`, so the represented Binaryen `Type::isSubType(curr->type, child->type)` decision now records nullable, exact, and heap mismatch outcomes before the child-cast plan consumes it instead of hiding that decision behind a helper-style predicate. This intentionally does not widen behavior and uses the existing `*ref.cast*` coverage as the guard. Descriptor child casts remain a documented boundary until Starshine has the child-localization payload needed to drop or reorder descriptor operands safely.

The 2026-07-07 ordinary `ref.cast` child-`ref.as_non_null` slice added `OiRefCastChildNonNullFact` so Binaryen v130 `visitRefCast` wrapper removal after known-result and child-cast folds is represented as a plan fact: if an ordinary parent cast sees a child `ref.as_non_null`, the parent rewires to the wrapper operand and retargets itself to the non-null version of the original cast type. Focused red-first coverage now proves a nullable struct cast over `ref.as_non_null(eqref)` keeps the trap-preserving `ref.cast` but removes the child wrapper.

The 2026-07-07 ordinary `ref.cast` fallthrough/GLB slice added `OiRefCastTighteningFact` so Binaryen v130 `visitRefCast` target improvement is represented before known-result and child-wrapper planning: ordinary casts intersect their current target with `getFallthroughType(ref)` via the shared ref fallthrough lower-bound fact, then either feed the tightened type to existing rewrite facts or rebuild the cast with the tightened target. Focused red-first coverage now proves `(ref.cast (ref null $foo) (local.get (ref eq)))` tightens to a non-null `$foo` target instead of preserving the nullable target.

The 2026-07-08 ordinary `ref.test` fallthrough/GLB slice added `OiRefTestTighteningFact` so Binaryen v130 `visitRefTest` target improvement is represented before known-result planning: ordinary tests intersect their current cast type with `getFallthroughType(ref)` via the shared ref fallthrough lower-bound fact, then either feed the tightened type to existing rewrite facts or rebuild the test with the narrowed target. Focused red-first coverage now proves `(ref.test (ref null struct) (local.get (ref eq)))` tightens the test immediate to non-null `structref` while preserving the runtime predicate because the result is still unknown. The follow-up fallthrough-miss slice added `OiRefProducerFact::misses_target` consumption in `OiRefTestOperandFact`, so Binaryen's `evaluateCastCheck(getFallthroughType(ref), castType)` failure path is represented for producer-only fallthrough misses such as a broad `eqref` block whose live fallthrough value is `i31ref` tested against non-null `structref`. The descriptor-test structure slice split descriptor-style `ref.test_desc` success / success-if-non-null evaluation into `OiDescriptorRefTestEvaluationFact`, preserving the current source-backed same-heap/subtype behavior without widening while leaving descriptor `ref.test_desc` GLB tightening and miss widening as documented reopeners. The follow-up tightening-structure slice split ordinary test GLB rewriting into `OiOrdinaryRefTestTighteningFact` and made the descriptor-test GLB gap an explicit `OiDescriptorRefTestTighteningFact` boundary-only fact; this intentionally preserves behavior because local descriptor-test validation still lacks a useful red-first GLB fixture for same-shape or bottom-target cases. The descriptor-test miss-boundary slice added `OiDescriptorRefTestMissFact` plus an invalid-shape regression documenting that Starshine validation rejects a disjoint `ref.test_desc` target with `ref.test_desc target does not match operand type` before OI can fold it; reopen descriptor-test miss widening only with a validated public/HOT fixture whose descriptor target can miss the operand type.

The 2026-07-08 descriptor `ref.cast` fallthrough slice added `OiDescriptorCastTighteningFact` and `OiDescriptorCastTighteningRewritePlanFact` so Binaryen v130 `visitRefCast` descriptor-cast nullability improvement is separate from descriptor success/exactness facts: a nullable descriptor cast whose reference operand has a non-null fallthrough type rebuilds as a non-null descriptor cast even when Starshine cannot prove the operand heap matches or subtypes the target heap. Focused red-first coverage now proves `(ref.cast_desc_eq (ref null $foo) (local.get (ref eq)) (local.get (ref $foo_desc)))` tightens to `(ref $foo)` rather than staying nullable.

The 2026-07-08 call_ref target skip slice added `OiCallRefTargetSkipNonNullFact` so Binaryen v130 `visitCallRef`'s pre-target `skipNonNullCast(curr->target, curr)` step is represented before direct/table/fallthrough/select target classification. The follow-up nullable-target slice widened that fact from statically non-null children to call_ref/return_call_ref final-target children, matching Binaryen's sibling-effect check: because the target is the final child, removing `ref.as_non_null` does not move its null trap past later sibling effects. Focused red-first coverage now proves `ref.as_non_null(table.get)` call_ref and return_call_ref targets lower to `call_indirect` / `return_call_indirect` instead of remaining indirect through `call_ref`, while broader non-final child cast skipping remains out of scope.

The 2026-07-08 raw flat pure-scalar atom structure slice added `RawOiFlatPureScalarLeafFact`, `RawOiFlatPureScalarUnaryOpFact`, and `RawOiFlatPureScalarBinaryOpFact` so the raw OI-G same-address `memory.copy` fallback parses bounded postfix address atoms and operations as fact records before forming `RawOiFlatPureScalarAddressFact`; the old leaf/unary/binary key helpers and commutativity helper were removed. The follow-up raw region structure slice added `RawOiFlatPureScalarBudgetFact` and `RawOiSameFlatPureScalarMemoryCopyRegionFact` so the accepted parser limits and recursive same-address rewrite traversal are fact-owned rather than `run_hot_pipeline_raw_oi_*` helper surfaces. The raw emission split then moved already-proven lowered-bulk operand-chunk emission into `RawOiBulkLoweringRewriteFact::append_operand_chunk` and same-address flat pure-scalar operand-drop emission into `RawOiFlatPureScalarAddressFact::append_dropped_operand`, leaving no emission-only `run_hot_pipeline_raw_oi_push_*` helpers. These intentionally preserve behavior and use existing focused memory-copy coverage because the structure splits only move represented parser limits, traversal, leaves, scalar unary/convert ops, integer/float binary ops, integer commutative canonicalization bits, and rewrite-payload copying into named facts.

The 2026-07-08 call_ref immediate-target structure slice added `OiCallRefDirectTargetFact` and `OiCallRefTableTargetFact` so the Binaryen v130 `visitCallRef` direct `RefFunc` and immediate `TableGet` paths are explicit facts consumed by `OiCallRefTargetFact`, not opcode-local branches inside the generic target classifier. This intentionally does not widen behavior: existing direct ref.func, table.get, return_call_ref, and ref.get_desc call_ref coverage already exercised the represented direct/table target behavior, and the slice only moved those proofs into named fact records.

The 2026-07-08 call_ref operand-interposition structure slice added `OiCallRefFallthroughOperandInterpositionFact` and `OiCallRefSelectResidueOperandInterpositionFact`, splitting Binaryen v130 `visitCallRef` / `CallUtils::convertToDirectCalls` argument-order preservation out of `OiCallRefOperandFact`: fallthrough-target directization owns `set(last); drop(target); get(last)`, and same-target select residue directization owns effectful condition/arm evaluation after the last operand before the final direct call. This intentionally does not widen behavior because existing call_ref fallthrough and same-target select coverage already exercised these represented order paths.

The 2026-07-08 call_ref result block-type structure slice added `OiCallRefResultBlockTypeFact`, replacing the generic call_ref result-block helper with a fact that records Binaryen v130 `curr->type` reconstruction for fallthrough-target and same-target-select residue wrappers. The represented HOT builder boundary remains void or single-result wrapper blocks; multivalue direct-call wrappers still require broader multivalue/localization repair facts before they can be widened. Existing focused `*call_ref*` coverage was used because this was a structure-first/no-widening split.

The 2026-07-09 call_ref result-arity structure follow-up added `OiCallRefResultArityFact` under `OiCallRefResultBlockTypeFact`, splitting the void-or-single-result proof from the optional HOT wrapper block type used by fallthrough and same-target-select residue directization. This is structure-only/no-widening: represented Binaryen v130 `curr->type` reconstruction still accepts only void and single-result wrappers, while multivalue call_ref localization/repair remains open. Existing focused `*call_ref*` coverage remains the behavior guard; no red-first test was added because behavior intentionally did not change.

The 2026-07-08 descriptor call_ref child-directization structure slice added `OiDescriptorCallRefDirectizationFact`, replacing the descriptor operand simplification plan's two boolean opcode checks with a fact over descriptor-cast operand and descriptor slots. The fact source-maps the Binaryen v130 visitor order where child `visitCallRef` directization can run before descriptor-cast cleanup; Starshine still invokes the same existing child directization prelude but now records which descriptor-cast children are call_ref producers as data before retrying descriptor skip/TNH/null-check movement plans. A follow-up no-widening split added `OiDescriptorCallRefDirectizationKind`, so operand-only, descriptor-only, and operand-plus-descriptor child-directization outcomes are explicit result kinds with optional payload ids instead of `-1` sentinel slots. The 2026-07-09 payload refinement then replaced that kind-plus-parallel-optionals encoding with ordered `OiDescriptorCallRefChildDirectizationFact` payloads: operand child first, descriptor child second when both qualify, and only a single descriptor payload when the descriptor slot is the only `call_ref`. A later descriptor operand-target relation split added `OiDescriptorOperandTargetRelationFact` so descriptor TNH skip and result narrowing consume one nested source/target relation fact instead of parallel operand match/nullability/exactness booleans. Existing focused `*call_ref*` and `*descriptor*` coverage was used because these were structure-first/no-widening splits.

The 2026-07-08 call_ref rewrite-application structure slice added `OiCallRefDirectizationFact` and `OiCallRefRewriteFact`, wrapping Binaryen v130 `visitCallRef`'s ordered target null-trap and direct/table/fallthrough/select directization sequence as a single fact-owned visitor record. The former call_ref visitor helper now only requests the rewrite fact and applies it; fallthrough replacement emission also moved under `OiCallRefDirectizePlanFact`. This intentionally preserves behavior and uses existing focused `*call_ref*` coverage because the slice only made the application order explicit after the already fact-backed target, operand, result-block, and null-trap records.

The 2026-07-08 call_ref ordered-target classification structure slice added `OiCallRefTargetClassificationFact` and moved select child-slot parsing to `OiCallRefSelectTargetFact::from_select`, so Binaryen v130 `visitCallRef`'s target order is represented as one fact record: direct `ref.func`, immediate `table.get`, fallthrough `ref.func`, then the `CallUtils::convertToDirectCalls` select route. `OiCallRefTargetFact` is now a projection target consumed from ordered classification facts rather than an entry point that reclassifies target expressions itself. A 2026-07-08 no-widening refinement changed `OiCallRefTargetClassificationFact` from a classification kind plus parallel optional payload fields to a single `classified_target_fact` projection, so the ordered classifier owns source order while downstream planning consumes one explicit target fact. This intentionally preserves behavior and relies on existing focused `*call_ref*` coverage rather than red-first tests because it only moves proof ownership.

The 2026-07-08 call_ref directization-plan target proof split added `OiCallRefDirectFuncPlanFact`, `OiCallRefTableTargetPlanFact`, and `OiCallRefFallthroughFuncPlanFact`, removing the remaining direct/table/fallthrough sentinel payload fields and `has_*` predicate checks from `OiCallRefTargetFact`. `OiCallRefDirectizePlanFact` now chooses and emits direct calls, table calls, and fallthrough direct calls by consuming the explicit target proof records above, preserving the same Binaryen v130 target order without widening behavior; existing focused `*call_ref*` coverage remains the behavior guard.

The 2026-07-08 call_ref invocation structure slice added `OiCallRefInvocationFact`, making Binaryen v130 `visitCallRef`'s child-slot layout explicit: all non-final children are operands, the final child is the source callee reference, target-slot `skipNonNullCast` chooses an effective callee, and `OiCallRefTargetClassificationFact` classifies that effective target before a directization plan is built. This removes the last directization-local target/argument split and the old target-fact reclassification wrapper without widening behavior; existing focused `*call_ref*` coverage was used for this structure-first split. The follow-up child-layout split added `OiCallRefChildLayoutFact`, moving that final-target/effective-target/argument layout under a shared fact consumed by both the null-trap plan and directization invocation; target null trapping now stops after the shared layout fact instead of recomputing target skip or running broader direct/table/fallthrough/select classification. This also intentionally preserves behavior and used existing focused `*call_ref*` coverage.

The 2026-07-08 call_ref fallthrough-direct structure slice added `OiCallRefFallthroughDirectTargetFact` so the Binaryen v130 `visitCallRef` `Properties::getFallthrough(curr->target)` direct-`ref.func` route and the target-static-heap versus fallthrough-`ref.func` heap compatibility gate are an explicit target fact consumed by `OiCallRefTargetFact`. A structure-only follow-up added `OiCallRefFallthroughDirectFuncFact` so loop/if/br_on fallthrough wrappers and `OiCallRefFallthroughDirectTargetFact` consume an explicit direct-`ref.func` proof instead of asking sentinel-style `has direct function` questions of the broader recursive fallthrough traversal record. The latest refinement moved that direct proof into an optional nested payload on `OiCallRefFallthroughTargetFact`, removing the remaining direct-function sentinel fields from the traversal record itself while preserving the same Binaryen v130 fallthrough-target behavior. A further no-widening refinement added `OiCallRefIfFallthroughArmChoiceFact` under `OiCallRefIfFallthroughTargetFact`, replacing stored then/else stop booleans with an explicit one-sided arm-choice fact for Binaryen v130 `Properties::getImmediateFallthrough` through if targets. This intentionally does not widen behavior: existing local.tee, ref.as_non_null, same-heap ref.cast, block, loop, if, br_on, and last-operand interposition call_ref coverage already exercised the represented fallthrough target behavior; the slices only removed the block-vs-generic fallthrough branches from the target classifier and record the proof in named facts.

The 2026-07-08 call_ref known-null target slices added `OiCallRefKnownNullTargetFact` and `OiCallRefNullTrapPlanFact` so Binaryen v130 `visitCallRef`'s `trapOnNull(curr, curr->target)` step is represented after target-slot non-null skipping and before direct/table/fallthrough/select classification. The target fact proves direct `ref.null` targets (including after the final-target `ref.as_non_null` skip), pure single-root block fallthroughs whose tail is `ref.null`, and branch-free effectful block targets whose fallthrough tail is `ref.null`; the plan preserves effectful call_ref arguments through `OiOrderedOperandFact`, then preserves target-block effects by dropping the whole target block before replacing the call_ref / return_call_ref with `unreachable`. Focused red-first public coverage now proves direct, pure fallthrough-known-null, and branch-free effectful fallthrough-known-null call_ref / return_call_ref targets no longer survive as indirect calls while argument and target effects remain before the trap; broader fallthrough-known-null target control/EH and escaping-branch localization remain reopenable gaps.

The 2026-07-08 call_ref fallthrough type slice added `OiCallRefFallthroughTypeFact` and extended `OiCallRefFallthroughTargetFact` through same-heap ordinary `ref.cast` wrappers. This mirrors Binaryen v130 `visitCallRef`: after `Properties::getFallthrough(curr->target)` exposes a `ref.func`, Starshine now directizes only when the original target expression's static heap matches the fallthrough `ref.func` heap. Focused red-first HOT coverage now proves a `local.tee(ref.func); ref.cast (ref null $sig); call_ref $sig` target becomes a drop-preserving direct call instead of remaining `call_ref`. The follow-up one-sided-if slice adds `OiCallRefIfFallthroughTargetFact` for Binaryen v130 `Properties::getImmediateFallthrough` through `if` targets with exactly one explicit unreachable arm; public red-first coverage now proves call_ref and return_call_ref drop the original `if` target and emit a direct call/return_call when the live arm falls through to `ref.func`, while two-live-arm control, branch/EH effects, and multivalue target localization remain reopeners. The structure-only arm-choice split adds `OiCallRefIfFallthroughArmChoiceFact`, preserving that represented one-sided-if behavior while recording whether the then or else arm is the explicit stop as data rather than carrying parallel stop booleans on the target fact. The follow-up loop-body slices add `OiCallRefLoopFallthroughTargetFact` for Binaryen v130 loop-body fallthrough; public red-first coverage now proves call_ref and return_call_ref drop single-root and multi-root loop targets and emit a direct call/return_call when the loop body tail falls through to `ref.func`, while loop-internal branch/EH exits and multivalue localization remain reopeners. The follow-up `br_on_*` slice adds `OiCallRefBrOnFallthroughTargetFact` for Binaryen v130 `Properties::getImmediateFallthroughPtr` returning `BrOn::ref`; focused red-first HOT coverage now proves call_ref and return_call_ref drop a target-side `br_on_null(ref.func)` branch evaluation before a direct call/return_call, while broader branch retargeting, branch-value localization, EH, and multivalue repair remain reopeners. A structure-only refinement then made the represented `br_on_*` kind, branch label, and final reference-child proof explicit in `OiCallRefBrOnFallthroughTargetFact`, with focused HOT guards for `br_on_non_null`, `br_on_cast`, and `br_on_cast_fail`; this intentionally preserves behavior and only tightens the fact record behind the existing target-drop path.

The 2026-07-08 call_ref select-arm wrapper slices widened `OiCallRefSelectArmFact` so the select-target classifier can look through no-op `ref.as_non_null` wrappers around direct `ref.func` arms and then added `OiCallRefSelectArmCastFact` for known-success same-heap ordinary `ref.cast(ref.func)` arm wrappers before lowering a select target to an `if` of direct calls / return_calls. The follow-up structure-only splits added `OiCallRefSelectArmDirectFact` and made `OiCallRefSelectArmFact` carry that fact as an optional nested payload, so the Binaryen v130 `CallUtils::convertToDirectCalls` known-direct-arm proof is a first-class fact consumed by wrapper/cast and select-target construction instead of repeated raw sentinel checks or `-1` payload fields. This mirrors Binaryen v130's child-visitor cleanup before `CallUtils::convertToDirectCalls` without claiming effectful arm fallthrough, nested-select, table, descriptor, or mismatched/unknown cast arm breadth. Focused coverage now proves both `select(ref.as_non_null(ref.func), ref.as_non_null(ref.func), cond)` and `select(ref.cast same-heap ref.func, ref.cast same-heap ref.func, cond)` call_ref targets directize to direct `if` calls and erase the wrappers/casts.

The 2026-07-08 call_ref same-target select slices split the select directization plan further: `OiCallRefSelectTargetFact` now owns the select-specific known-arm functions, same-target proof, condition proof, and residue arm id under `OiCallRefTargetFact`, while `OiCallRefDirectizePlanFact` routes identical known `ref.func` arms to a one-call replacement instead of an `if` with duplicate calls. The follow-up `OiCallRefSelectConditionFact` makes the select condition's i32 type and effect-preservation decision explicit: pure conditions are erased with the duplicate target arms, while effectful conditions are interposed at Binaryen's target-evaluation slot after the last call_ref operand and before the direct call. The 2026-07-08 residue split added `OiCallRefSelectTargetResidueFact`, so the effectful same-target path now owns the Binaryen-style dropped target evaluation (`drop(block(drop(condition), proven-target-arm))`) separately from operand placement. The latest structure-only split adds `OiCallRefSelectSameTargetFact` and `OiCallRefSelectDirectCallsFact` so Binaryen v130 `CallUtils::convertToDirectCalls` identical-arm and two-direct-call select target proofs are explicit fact records rather than sentinel-style `has_*` checks on the broader select-target record. This mirrors the represented Binaryen v130 `CallUtils::convertToDirectCalls` same-target and two-direct-arm paths while keeping nested selects, mixed known/unknown arms, target-side control/EH effects, and multivalue/localization as separate ChildLocalizer/order-sensitive reopeners. Focused coverage now proves both pure scalar-argument same-`ref.func` selects directize to one clean call and effectful-condition same-target selects preserve a dropped target-residue block before the direct call while erasing `call_ref`, `select`, and the unnecessary `if`.

The 2026-07-09 call_ref select-condition type follow-up added `OiCallRefSelectConditionTypeFact` under `OiCallRefSelectConditionFact`, splitting the single-i32 condition proof from the condition effect-preservation payload before `CallUtils::convertToDirectCalls` select directization builds either a same-target residue or a two-direct-call `if`. This is structure-only/no-widening: represented direct-arm select targets still require the same live i32 condition, preserve effectful conditions in the same target-evaluation slot, and leave nested/mixed/control/EH/multivalue select directization reopeners unchanged.

The 2026-07-09 call_ref select-condition effect structure slice split `OiCallRefSelectConditionFact` again so the condition fact owns the typed i32 child while `OiCallRefSelectConditionEffectFact` and `OiCallRefSelectConditionPreserveEffectsFact` own the Binaryen v130 `CallUtils::convertToDirectCalls` pure-erasure versus preserve-by-drop decision. This is structure-only/no-widening: effect-free same-target select conditions still disappear with the duplicate arms, effectful conditions still materialize through `OiCallRefSelectTargetResidueFact` as `drop(block(drop(condition), proven-target-arm))`, and the broader nested/mixed/control/EH/multivalue select directization reopeners remain unchanged.

The 2026-07-07 `ref.is_null` TNH skipCast slice added `OiRefIsNullSkipCastFact` so Binaryen v130 `visitRefIsNull` nullable `ref.cast` removal under `--traps-never-happen` is represented as a fact-driven plan after direct known-null/non-null folds; focused red-first coverage now proves default mode preserves the potentially trapping nullable cast while TNH erases it and keeps the null predicate. The preceding `ref.is_null` routing slice moved direct `RefIsNull` folding behind `OiRefIsNullFact` and `OiRefIsNullRewritePlanFact`, and moved `ref.test` / `ref.eq` emission of `ref.is_null` through fact-owned plan methods, removing the last `optimize_instructions_*is*` helper-level proof surfaces. Before that, the 2026-07-07 heap/remainder boundary slice made the remaining relation primitives fact-owned without widening behavior: `OiHeapSubtypeFact` owns the bounded module-subtype proof consumed by `OiHeapRelationFact`, `OiConcreteSourceTargetOverlapFact` owns the declared-subtype no-overlap walk used for known-miss cast/test decisions, and `OiFinalHeapFact` owns the concrete-final heap proof for exact/final reference tests. `OiRemainderInstructionFact` owns the liveness plus direct/local.tee integer-remainder shape that keeps compare-to-zero cleanup trap-preserving, and `OiUnsupportedAggregateAtomicReceiverFact` names the current fail-closed aggregate-atomic representation blocker instead of leaving it as a top-level helper predicate. The remaining `ref.is_null` emission is an associated fact-plan method used after `OiRefTestRewritePlanFact`, `OiRefEqRelationFact`, or `OiRefIsNullRewritePlanFact` has already proven the rewrite; reopen this boundary if child-count, operand purity, known-null/non-null, TNH skipCast, or target proof logic reappears outside those facts.

The 2026-07-09 ref.eq i31 non-null/disjoint structure slice added `OiRefEqI31NonNullFact` / `OiRefEqI31NonNullKind` and `OiRefEqI31DisjointTargetFact` / `OiRefEqI31DisjointTargetKind` under `OiRefEqI31Fact`, replacing direct known-non-null and cannot-match booleans with selected Binaryen v130 `visitRefEq` i31 local/literal and disjoint-target proofs. This intentionally widens no behavior: represented i31-vs-disjoint-heap false rewrites still require the same known-non-null i31 side and the same local target heap that cannot match i31 before preserving effects and emitting `i32.const 0`. Existing focused `*ref.eq*` OI coverage remains the behavior guard, and broader reference/descriptor/null-trap fact breadth remains open.

The 2026-07-09 array storage-default structure slice added `OiArrayStorageDefaultValueKind` under `OiArrayStorageDefaultValueFact`, replacing the direct storage-default boolean with selected i32/i64/f32/f64 zero-default, nullable-ref-null-default, and non-default outcomes. This intentionally widens no behavior: represented `array.new` and repeated `array.new_fixed` default detection still accepts the same direct zero constants and nullable ref.null leaves after the same fallthrough traversal, while broader SIMD defaults, packed/reference edge breadth, and control/EH/multivalue localization remain open.

The 2026-07-09 array default-value structure slice added `OiArrayDefaultValueKind` under `OiArrayDefaultValueFact`, replacing the direct initializer-default boolean with selected no-module-context, missing-field, storage-nondefault, and storage-default outcomes. This intentionally widens no behavior: represented `array.new` and repeated `array.new_fixed` constructor planning still uses the same fallthrough traversal, storage-default proof, and dropped-child preservation plan before choosing default versus non-default rewrites; broader ChildLocalizer control/EH/multivalue and SIMD default breadth remain open.

The 2026-07-09 array.new_fixed representative-default structure slice added `OiArrayNewFixedRepresentativeDefaultFact` / `OiArrayNewFixedRepresentativeDefaultKind` under `OiArrayNewFixedRepeatedValueFact`, replacing the direct representative-default boolean with selected default and non-default representative outcomes backed by the array default-value fact. This intentionally widens no behavior: default repeated fixed-array representatives still select `array.new_default` with the same dropped-child preservation plan, while non-default representatives still use the same localization and `array.new` rewrite paths; broader ChildLocalizer control/EH/multivalue breadth remains open.

The 2026-07-09 array length trap-budget fact was superseded and deleted on 2026-07-11. Binaryen v130's direct `visitArrayLen`, `visitArrayGet`, and `visitArraySet` implementations do not inspect any fresh constructor, so a pass-local allocation-size threshold was not a valid consumer admission fact. Focused `*array*` OI coverage now preserves fixed/default/repeated constructors across ordinary, packed, effectful, in-bounds, out-of-bounds, and allocation-trap cases.

## What upstream Binaryen still does that Starshine lacks

The local pass does not yet model the upstream visitor families for:

- broad reference-typed and GC rewrites beyond the many narrow OI-I/OI-J/OI-K subsets already covered; OI-J now covers direct-call exact descriptor misses with ordered nontrapping local/scalar-constant/global arguments, pure-reference/direct-descriptor-call exact descriptor misses with ordered nontrapping local/scalar-constant/global descriptor arguments plus branch-free value-block, no-parameter direct value-call, parameterized direct value-call descriptor-call arguments with ordered nontrapping leaf operands, no-parameter direct non-null reference-result descriptor-call arguments, parameterized direct non-null reference-result descriptor-call arguments with nontrapping leaf operands, scalar-producer local.tee descriptor-call arguments, pure nontrapping-leaf select descriptor-call arguments, stack-form trapping integer div/rem scalar descriptor-call arguments with nontrapping leaves, and exact `ref.func` + `call_ref` descriptor producers, pure-local direct-call exact descriptor successes plus a Binaryen-backed keep-spelling boundary for scalar-constant/global exact-success direct-call arguments, typed-table call_ref reference-producer exact descriptor successes and descriptor-producer exact-successes under TNH after directization to call_indirect, typed-table call_ref descriptor-producer strict-subtype misses directized to call_indirect, same-heap direct-call descriptor exactification/narrowing with ordered nontrapping local/scalar-constant/global arguments, standalone `ref.get_desc` null-check movement through direct local, nullable global.get, local.tee(local.get/global.get), branch-free block, self-contained branch/cast block, escaping direct-`br` and value-`br_table` block children, branch-free select, - tuple extraction parity beyond the one-use tuple.make subset with pure siblings or covered selected trapping lanes (including earlier/later, two-later, two-earlier, and two-earlier-plus-one/two/three/four/five/six/seven/eight-later effectful sibling coverage) and single-result effectful/trapping sibling drop/localization; the covered one-use subset now routes through explicit `OiTupleExtractStructuralFact` / `OiTupleExtractTupleMakePayloadFact` structural outcomes, `OiTupleLaneLocalizeFact`, `OiTupleLaneTrapFact`, `OiTupleLaneDiscardFact`, `OiTupleLaneMaterializeFact`, `OiTupleLaneFact`, and `OiTupleExtractFact` lane facts plus `OiTupleSiblingEffectFact` preserved-sibling order facts, `OiTupleSelectedMaterializeFact` selected-lane capture/reload facts, `OiTupleExtractRewritePlanFact` direct-forward/materialize rewrite plans, and shared `OiOrderedOperandFact` scalar effect-order facts instead of the old open-coded tuple scanner, but full `simplify-locals` and dedicated `tuple-optimization` on public multivalue-block probes, including effect-count ladder coverage through ninety-seven later non-selected effects for `tuple-optimization` variants, are documented boundaries because Binaryen uses tuple scratch and Starshine keeps the block/drop spelling, direct-HOT replay of the full-simplify shape currently hits `InvalidChildRef`, local-carried / multi-use tuple extraction is a documented keep-spelling boundary for the probed Binaryen `version_130` shape, and multi-result non-selected siblings (including the earlier-sibling variant) plus multi-result selected children, including the selected-second, selected-third, selected-fourth, selected-fifth, selected-sixth, selected-seventh, selected-eighth, selected-ninth, selected-tenth, selected-eleventh, selected-twelfth, selected-thirteenth, and selected-fourteenth lanes, remain broader tuple-scratch localization boundaries, while the direct no-sibling selected-fifteenth, selected-sixteenth, selected-seventeenth, selected-eighteenth, and selected-nineteenth call shapes are source-backed keep-spelling boundaries
- a complete whole-function local prescan equivalent beyond the current Binaryen-shaped integer local fact store: Starshine now has per-local sign-extension and unsigned-max facts for direct/local-carried sign and maxBits folds, with `OiSignExtValueFact` / `OiUnsignedMaxValueFact` owning the assignment-value and local-get consumer classification plus the represented `and`/`or`/`xor`/`shr_u`, arithmetic `add`/`mul`/effective constant-`shl`/effective constant-`shr_s`/div/rem, unsigned-load, and boolean compare/`eqz` maxBits subset and `OiEqzWrapI64MaxBitsFact` / `OiExtendWrapI64MaxBitsFact` / `OiZeroBitsReplacementFact` consuming that fact for the Binaryen eqz-wrap, extend-wrap, and pure zero-bit replacement rewrites; `OiI32EffectiveShiftAmountFact` / `OiI64EffectiveShiftAmountFact` own masked negative/out-of-range constant shift amounts and `OiCombinedShiftZeroBitsFact` owns the narrow post-combine logical-shift zero result. The pass still lacks full upstream `Bits::getMaxBits` breadth over select, arbitrary fallthrough/control expressions, effect-preserving non-pure zero-bit replacement, more precise helper-backed local facts for newer locals added after scanning, and the rest of Binaryen's source-level helper lattice. Direct, `i32.wrap_i64`, `i64.extend_i32_u`, eqz-wrap, extend-wrap, arithmetic add/mul/effective-shl/effective-shr_s/div/rem maxBits, boolean compare/`eqz`, and pure zero-bit maxBits compare folds/spelling/replacement rewrites including narrowed child facts, direct sign-extension equality range folds plus unsigned-top compare facts (`OiI32SignExtensionRangeFact`, `OiI32SignExtensionEqualityFoldFact`, `OiI32SignExtensionUnsignedTopCompareFact`, and `OiI64SignExtensionUnsignedTopCompareFact`), and source-backed sign-extension relational plus i32/i64 dynamic-shift maxBits keep-spelling boundaries remain the documented covered/boundary subset rather than full LocalScanner parity.
- deferred `ReFinalize` / final optimizer / EH-pop repair inside this pass is a documented representation blocker, not an accepted semantic gap: Binaryen v130 sets a pass-local `refinalize` flag when replacements or GC/reference rewrites change expression types, then runs `ReFinalize`, a pass-local `FinalOptimizer`, and `EHUtils::handleBlockNestedPops`; Starshine OI currently constructs typed HOT replacements directly and has catch regions / catch-info side tables but no first-class Binaryen-style EH `pop` node to repair. Reopen this only with a HOT/raw EH payload-pop fact surface, a safe post-OI refinalization API, or a reduced source-backed mismatch requiring the Binaryen final repair phase inside OI.

The 2026-06-19 `version_130` matrix routes those gaps to `[O4Z-AUDIT-OI-D]` through `[O4Z-AUDIT-OI-M]`, with `[O4Z-AUDIT-OI-N]` reserved for final direct/O4z closeout. That gap is intentional and documented so readers do not mistake the current local pass for a full upstream port.

## How to read this with the rest of the folder

- [`./index.md`](./index.md) explains the overall pass role and page map.
- [`./binaryen-strategy.md`](./binaryen-strategy.md) explains the upstream Binaryen contract.
- [`./implementation-structure-and-tests.md`](./implementation-structure-and-tests.md) maps the owning files and proof surfaces.
- [`./gc-casts-call_ref-and-trap-sensitive-rewrites.md`](./gc-casts-call_ref-and-trap-sensitive-rewrites.md) covers the upstream reference-typed half that the current local pass does not model.
- [`./wat-shapes.md`](./wat-shapes.md) gives the beginner-friendly shape catalog.
- [`./starshine-hot-ir-strategy.md`](./starshine-hot-ir-strategy.md) is the exact MoonBit helper/code-map companion.

## Validation guidance

The current local evidence surface is:

- focused WAT tests for the exact families listed above,
- registry and explicit-pass CLI tests proving `optimize-instructions` remains active,
- repeated-pass replay coverage on the debug artifact and ordered generated-artifact predecessors, and
- pass-targeted fuzz comparison when the implementation changes.

That is enough to keep the current HOT subset honest while preserving the distinction between local reality and upstream Binaryen's wider pass contract.
